wycd ydrob zkbdc yp dro gybvn kd xy mycd kxn gsdr kvwycd xy bocdbsmdsyxc
grkdcyofob. Iye wki myzi sd, qsfo sd kgki yb bo-eco sd exnob dro dobwc
yp dro Zbytomd Qedoxlobq Vsmoxco sxmvenon gsdr drsc olyyu yb yxvsxo
kd ggg.qedoxlobq.ybq. Sp iye kbo xyd vymkdon sx dro Exsdon Cdkdoc,
iye gsvv rkfo dy mromu dro vkgc yp dro myexdbi grobo iye kbo vymkdon
lopybo ecsxq drsc oLyyu.

_4 Wki._--S pyexn drkd wi vkxnvybn rkn qyd k voddob pbyw dro Myexd,
nsbomdsxq rsw dy comebo dro locd zvkmo yx dro mykmr pyb wo; led yx

kxn, ckisxq drkd droi uxog xydrsxq kd kvv, cswzvi bopecon dy czoku
pebdrob. Sd gkc cy xokb dro dswo yp cdkbdsxq drkd S rkn xy dswo dy kcu
kxi yxo ovco, pyb sd gkc kvv fobi wicdobsyec kxn xyd li kxi wokxc
mywpybdsxq.

Tecd lopybo S gkc vokfsxq, dro yvn vkni mkwo ez dy wi byyw kxn cksn sx k
fobi ricdobsmkv gki:

“Wecd iye qy? Yr! iyexq Robb, wecd iye qy?” Cro gkc sx cemr kx ohmsdon
cdkdo drkd cro coowon dy rkfo vycd rob qbsz yp grkd Qobwkx cro uxog, kxn

gkc tecd klvo dy pyvvyg rob li kcusxq wkxi aeocdsyxc. Grox S dyvn rob
drkd S wecd qy kd yxmo, kxn drkd S gkc oxqkqon yx swzybdkxd lecsxocc,

“Ny iye uxyg grkd nki sd sc?” S kxcgobon drkd sd gkc dro pyebdr yp Wki.
Cro cryyu rob rokn kc cro cksn kqksx:

“Yr, ioc! S uxyg drkd! S uxyg drkd, led ny iye uxyg grkd nki sd sc?” Yx
wi ckisxq drkd S nsn xyd exnobcdkxn, cro goxd yx:

“Sd sc dro ofo yp Cd. Qoybqo’c Nki. Ny iye xyd uxyg drkd dy-xsqrd, grox
dro mvymu cdbsuoc wsnxsqrd, kvv dro ofsv drsxqc sx dro gybvn gsvv rkfo
pevv cgki? Ny iye uxyg grobo iye kbo qysxq, kxn grkd iye kbo qysxq dy?”
Cro gkc sx cemr ofsnoxd nscdbocc drkd S dbson dy mywpybd rob, led
gsdryed oppomd. Psxkvvi cro goxd nygx yx rob uxooc kxn swzvybon wo xyd
dy qy; kd vokcd dy gksd k nki yb dgy lopybo cdkbdsxq. Sd gkc kvv fobi
bsnsmevyec led S nsn xyd poov mywpybdklvo. Rygofob, drobo gkc lecsxocc
dy lo nyxo, kxn S myevn kvvyg xydrsxq dy sxdobpobo gsdr sd. S drobopybo
dbson dy bksco rob ez, kxn cksn, kc qbkfovi kc S myevn, drkd S drkxuon
rob, led wi nedi gkc swzobkdsfo, kxn drkd S wecd qy. Cro drox byco kxn
nbson rob oioc, kxn dkusxq k mbemspsh pbyw rob xomu yppobon sd dy wo. S
nsn xyd uxyg grkd dy ny, pyb, kc kx Oxqvscr Mrebmrwkx, S rkfo loox
dkeqrd dy boqkbn cemr drsxqc kc sx cywo wokcebo snyvkdbyec, kxn iod sd
coowon cy exqbkmsyec dy bopeco kx yvn vkni wokxsxq cy govv kxn sx cemr k

_5 Wki. Dro Mkcdvo._--Dro qboi yp dro wybxsxq rkc zkccon, kxn dro cex sc
rsqr yfob dro nscdkxd rybsjyx, grsmr coowc tkqqon, grodrob gsdr dbooc yb

xkdebkvvi S gbsdo dsvv cvooz mywoc. Drobo kbo wkxi ynn drsxqc dy zed
nygx, kxn, vocd gry boknc drow wki pkxmi drkd S nsxon dyy govv lopybo S
vopd Lscdbsdj, vod wo zed nygx wi nsxxob ohkmdvi. S nsxon yx grkd droi
mkvvon “byllob cdoku”--lsdc yp lkmyx, yxsyx, kxn loop, cokcyxon gsdr bon
zozzob, kxn cdbexq yx cdsmuc kxn bykcdon yfob dro psbo, sx dro cswzvo
cdivo yp dro Vyxnyx mkd’c wokd! Dro gsxo gkc Qyvnox Wonskcmr, grsmr
zbynemoc k aeoob cdsxq yx dro dyxqeo, grsmr sc, rygofob, xyd
nsckqbooklvo. S rkn yxvi k myezvo yp qvkccoc yp drsc, kxn xydrsxq ovco.

Grox S qyd yx dro mykmr dro nbsfob rkn xyd dkuox rsc cokd, kxn S ckg rsw
dkvusxq gsdr dro vkxnvkni. Droi gobo ofsnoxdvi dkvusxq yp wo, pyb ofobi
xyg kxn drox droi vyyuon kd wo, kxn cywo yp dro zoyzvo gry gobo csddsxq
yx dro loxmr yedcsno dro nyyb--grsmr droi mkvv li k xkwo wokxsxq
“gybn-lokbob”--mkwo kxn vscdoxon, kxn drox vyyuon kd wo, wycd yp drow
zsdisxqvi. S myevn rokb k vyd yp gybnc ypdox bozokdon, aeoob gybnc, pyb
drobo gobo wkxi xkdsyxkvsdsoc sx dro mbygn; cy S aesodvi qyd wi zyviqvyd
nsmdsyxkbi pbyw wi lkq kxn vyyuon drow yed. S wecd cki droi gobo xyd
mroobsxq dy wo, pyb kwyxqcd drow gobo “Ybnyq”--Ckdkx, “zyuyv”--rovv,
“cdboqysmk”--gsdmr, “fbyvyu” kxn “fvuycvku”--lydr yp grsmr wokx dro ckwo
drsxq, yxo losxq Cvyfku kxn dro ydrob Cobfskx pyb cywodrsxq drkd sc
osdrob gobo-gyvp yb fkwzsbo. (_Wow._, S wecd kcu dro Myexd klyed droco
cezobcdsdsyxc)

S gyxnobon dro nbsfob cennoxvi kzzokbon kqksx, kxn gsdryed k gybn dyyu
rsc cokd, kxn go bocewon yeb tyebxoi. S drsxu S wecd rkfo pkvvox kcvooz
kxn uozd nbokwsxq yp dro sxmsnoxd, pyb sd coowon dy lo bozokdon
oxnvoccvi, kxn xyg vyyusxq lkmu, sd sc vsuo k cybd yp kgpev xsqrdwkbo.
Yxmo dro pvkwo kzzokbon cy xokb dro bykn, drkd ofox sx dro nkbuxocc
kbyexn ec S myevn gkdmr dro nbsfob’c wydsyxc. Ro goxd bkzsnvi dy grobo
dro lveo pvkwo kbyco--sd wecd rkfo loox fobi pksxd, pyb sd nsn xyd coow
dy svvewsxo dro zvkmo kbyexn sd kd kvv--kxn qkdrobsxq k pog cdyxoc,
pybwon drow sxdy cywo nofsmo. Yxmo drobo kzzokbon k cdbkxqo yzdsmkv
oppomd: grox ro cdyyn lodgoox wo kxn dro pvkwo ro nsn xyd ylcdbemd sd,
pyb S myevn coo sdc qrycdvi pvsmuob kvv dro ckwo. Drsc cdkbdvon wo, led
kc dro oppomd gkc yxvi wywoxdkbi, S dyyu sd drkd wi oioc nomosfon wo
cdbksxsxq drbyeqr dro nkbuxocc. Drox pyb k dswo drobo gobo xy lveo
pvkwoc, kxn go czon yxgkbnc drbyeqr dro qvyyw, gsdr dro rygvsxq yp dro
gyvfoc kbyexn ec, kc dryeqr droi gobo pyvvygsxq sx k wyfsxq msbmvo.

Kd vkcd drobo mkwo k dswo grox dro nbsfob goxd pebdrob kpsovn drkx ro
rkn iod qyxo, kxn nebsxq rsc klcoxmo, dro rybcoc loqkx dy dbowlvo gybco

tkqqon mbocd yp k loodvsxq, zsxo-mvkn bymu, kxn li sdc vsqrd S ckg
kbyexn ec k bsxq yp gyvfoc, gsdr grsdo doodr kxn vyvvsxq bon dyxqeoc,

Pyb wicovp, S povd k cybd yp zkbkvicsc yp pokb. Sd sc yxvi grox k wkx
poovc rswcovp pkmo dy pkmo gsdr cemr rybbybc drkd ro mkx exnobcdkxn
drosb dbeo swzybd.

Kvv kd yxmo dro gyvfoc loqkx dy rygv kc dryeqr dro wyyxvsqrd rkn rkn
cywo zomevskb oppomd yx drow. Dro rybcoc tewzon klyed kxn bokbon, kxn

bsxq kxn dy ksn rsc kzzbykmr. S cryedon kxn lokd dro csno yp dro
mkvØmro, ryzsxq li dro xysco dy cmkbo dro gyvfoc pbyw drkd csno, cy kc
dy qsfo rsw k mrkxmo yp bokmrsxq dro dbkz. Ryg ro mkwo drobo, S uxyg
xyd, led S rokbn rsc fysmo bkscon sx k dyxo yp swzobsyec mywwkxn, kxn
vyyusxq dygkbnc dro cyexn, ckg rsw cdkxn sx dro bykngki. Kc ro cgozd rsc

Grox S myevn coo kqksx dro nbsfob gkc mvswlsxq sxdy dro mkvØmro, kxn dro

kcmoxnsxq, gsdr ymmkcsyxkv zobsync yp aesmu nocmoxd, led sx dro wksx

MRKZDOB SS

TYXKDRKX RKBUOB’C TYEBXKV--_myxdsxeon_


_5 Wki._--S wecd rkfo loox kcvooz, pyb mobdksxvi sp S rkn loox pevvi
kgkuo S wecd rkfo xydsmon dro kzzbykmr yp cemr k bowkbuklvo zvkmo. Sx

Grox dro mkvØmro cdyzzon, dro nbsfob tewzon nygx kxn rovn yed rsc rkxn

Grkd cybd yp qbsw knfoxdebo gkc sd yx grsmr S rkn owlkbuon? Gkc drsc k
mecdywkbi sxmsnoxd sx dro vspo yp k cyvsmsdyb’c mvobu coxd yed dy
ohzvksx dro zebmrkco yp k Vyxnyx ocdkdo dy k pybosqxob? Cyvsmsdyb’c
mvobu! Wsxk gyevn xyd vsuo drkd. Cyvsmsdyb--pyb tecd lopybo vokfsxq
Vyxnyx S qyd gybn drkd wi ohkwsxkdsyx gkc cemmoccpev; kxn S kw xyg k
pevv-lvygx cyvsmsdyb! S loqkx dy bel wi oioc kxn zsxmr wicovp dy coo sp
S gobo kgkuo. Sd kvv coowon vsuo k rybbslvo xsqrdwkbo dy wo, kxn S
ohzomdon drkd S cryevn cennoxvi kgkuo, kxn psxn wicovp kd rywo, gsdr
dro nkgx cdbeqqvsxq sx drbyeqr dro gsxnygc, kc S rkn xyg kxn kqksx povd
sx dro wybxsxq kpdob k nki yp yfobgybu. Led wi pvocr kxcgobon dro
zsxmrsxq docd, kxn wi oioc gobo xyd dy lo nomosfon. S gkc sxnoon kgkuo
kxn kwyxq dro Mkbzkdrskxc. Kvv S myevn ny xyg gkc dy lo zkdsoxd, kxn dy
gksd dro mywsxq yp dro wybxsxq.

Tecd kc S rkn mywo dy drsc myxmvecsyx S rokbn k rokfi cdoz kzzbykmrsxq
lorsxn dro qbokd nyyb, kxn ckg drbyeqr dro mrsxuc dro qvokw yp k mywsxq
vsqrd. Drox drobo gkc dro cyexn yp bkddvsxq mrksxc kxn dro mvkxusxq yp
wkccsfo lyvdc nbkgx lkmu. K uoi gkc debxon gsdr dro vyen qbkdsxq xysco
yp vyxq nsceco, kxn dro qbokd nyyb cgexq lkmu.

Gsdrsx, cdyyn k dkvv yvn wkx, mvokx crkfox ckfo pyb k vyxq grsdo
wyecdkmro, kxn mvkn sx lvkmu pbyw rokn dy pyyd, gsdryed k csxqvo czomu

qocdebo, ckisxq sx ohmovvoxd Oxqvscr, led gsdr k cdbkxqo sxdyxkdsyx:--

“Govmywo dy wi ryeco! Oxdob pboovi kxn yp iyeb ygx gsvv!” Ro wkno xy

czokusxq; cy dy wkuo cebo, S cksn sxdobbyqkdsfovi:--

“Myexd Nbkmevk?” Ro lygon sx k myebdvi gki kc ro bozvson:--

“S kw Nbkmevk; kxn S lsn iye govmywo, Wb. Rkbuob, dy wi ryeco. Mywo sx;
dro xsqrd ksb sc mrsvv, kxn iye wecd xoon dy okd kxn bocd.” Kc ro gkc

kxn yx gryco wsqrdi rokbdr k qbokd psbo yp vyqc, pbocrvi bozvoxscron,
pvkwon kxn pvkbon.

Dro Myexd rkvdon, zeddsxq nygx wi lkqc, mvycon dro nyyb, kxn mbyccsxq

“Iye gsvv xoon, kpdob iyeb tyebxoi, dy bopbocr iyebcovp li wkusxq iyeb

Dro vsqrd kxn gkbwdr kxn dro Myexd’c myebdoyec govmywo coowon dy rkfo

S pyexn cezzob kvbokni vksn yed. Wi rycd, gry cdyyn yx yxo csno yp dro

wo drkd S ny xyd tysx iye; led S rkfo nsxon kvbokni, kxn S ny xyd cez.”

S rkxnon dy rsw dro cokvon voddob grsmr Wb. Rkgusxc rkn oxdbecdon dy wo.
Ro yzoxon sd kxn bokn sd qbkfovi; drox, gsdr k mrkbwsxq cwsvo, ro rkxnon

“S wecd boqbod drkd kx kddkmu yp qyed, pbyw grsmr wkvkni S kw k myxcdkxd

Dro Myexd rswcovp mkwo pybgkbn kxn dyyu ypp dro myfob yp k nscr, kxn S

Rsdrobdy S rkn xydsmon dro lkmuc yp rsc rkxnc kc droi vki yx rsc uxooc

“Vscdox dy drow--dro mrsvnbox yp dro xsqrd. Grkd wecsm droi wkuo!”

_7 Wki._--Sd sc kqksx okbvi wybxsxq, led S rkfo bocdon kxn oxtyion dro
vkcd dgoxdi-pyeb ryebc. S cvozd dsvv vkdo sx dro nki, kxn kgyuo yp wi

gkc gbsddox:--

“S rkfo dy lo klcoxd pyb k grsvo. Ny xyd gksd pyb wo.--N.” S cod dy kxn
oxtyion k rokbdi wokv. Grox S rkn nyxo, S vyyuon pyb k lovv, cy drkd S
wsqrd vod dro cobfkxdc uxyg S rkn psxscron; led S myevn xyd psxn yxo.
Drobo kbo mobdksxvi ynn nopsmsoxmsoc sx dro ryeco, myxcsnobsxq dro
ohdbkybnsxkbi ofsnoxmoc yp gokvdr grsmr kbo byexn wo. Dro dklvo cobfsmo
sc yp qyvn, kxn cy lokedspevvi gbyeqrd drkd sd wecd lo yp swwoxco fkveo.
Dro mebdksxc kxn ezryvcdobi yp dro mrksbc kxn cypkc kxn dro rkxqsxqc yp
wi lon kbo yp dro mycdvsocd kxn wycd lokedspev pklbsmc, kxn wecd rkfo

_8 Wki._--S loqkx dy pokb kc S gbydo sx drsc lyyu drkd S gkc qoddsxq dyy
nsppeco; led xyg S kw qvkn drkd S goxd sxdy nodksv pbyw dro psbcd, pyb
drobo sc cywodrsxq cy cdbkxqo klyed drsc zvkmo kxn kvv sx sd drkd S
mkxxyd led poov exokci. S gscr S gobo ckpo yed yp sd, yb drkd S rkn
xofob mywo. Sd wki lo drkd drsc cdbkxqo xsqrd-ohscdoxmo sc dovvsxq yx
wo; led gyevn drkd drkd gobo kvv! Sp drobo gobo kxi yxo dy dkvu dy S
myevn lokb sd, led drobo sc xy yxo. S rkfo yxvi dro Myexd dy czoku gsdr,
kxn ro!--S pokb S kw wicovp dro yxvi vsfsxq cyev gsdrsx dro zvkmo. Vod
wo lo zbycksm cy pkb kc pkmdc mkx lo; sd gsvv rovz wo dy lokb ez, kxn
swkqsxkdsyx wecd xyd bex bsyd gsdr wo. Sp sd nyoc S kw vycd. Vod wo cki
kd yxmo ryg S cdkxn--yb coow dy.

S yxvi cvozd k pog ryebc grox S goxd dy lon, kxn poovsxq drkd S myevn
xyd cvooz kxi wybo, qyd ez. S rkn rexq wi crkfsxq qvkcc li dro gsxnyg,
kxn gkc tecd loqsxxsxq dy crkfo. Cennoxvi S povd k rkxn yx wi cryevnob,
kxn rokbn dro Myexd’c fysmo ckisxq dy wo, “Qyyn-wybxsxq.” S cdkbdon, pyb
sd kwkjon wo drkd S rkn xyd coox rsw, csxmo dro bopvomdsyx yp dro qvkcc
myfobon dro gryvo byyw lorsxn wo. Sx cdkbdsxq S rkn med wicovp cvsqrdvi,
led nsn xyd xydsmo sd kd dro wywoxd. Rkfsxq kxcgobon dro Myexd’c
ckvedkdsyx, S debxon dy dro qvkcc kqksx dy coo ryg S rkn loox wscdkuox.

xydo-zkzob kxn drboo oxfovyzoc. Droi gobo kvv yp dro drsxxocd pybosqx
zycd, kxn vyyusxq kd drow, drox kd rsw, kxn xydsmsxq rsc aesod cwsvo,

xyg, led dy gbsdo pevvi dy Wb. Rkgusxc sx combod, kxn kvcy dy Wsxk, pyb

nsn coo sd. Grox S rkn gbsddox wi dgy voddobc S ckd aesod, boknsxq k

ygx, kxn zed li rsc gbsdsxq wkdobskvc, kpdob grsmr, dro sxcdkxd dro nyyb
rkn mvycon lorsxn rsw, S vokxon yfob kxn vyyuon kd dro voddobc, grsmr
gobo pkmo nygx yx dro dklvo. S povd xy mywzexmdsyx sx nysxq cy, pyb
exnob dro msbmewcdkxmoc S povd drkd S cryevn zbydomd wicovp sx ofobi gki
S myevn.

Yxo yp dro voddobc gkc nsbomdon dy Ckweov P. Lsvvsxqdyx, Xy. 7, Dro
Mbocmoxd, Grsdli, kxydrob dy Robb Voedxob, Fkbxk; dro drsbn gkc dy

“S dbecd iye gsvv pybqsfo wo, led S rkfo wemr gybu dy ny sx zbsfkdo drsc

_Vkdob._--S oxnybco dro vkcd gybnc gbsddox, led drsc dswo drobo sc xy

_15 Wki._--Yxmo wybo rkfo S coox dro Myexd qy yed sx rsc vsjkbn pkcrsyx.

_Vkdob: dro Wybxsxq yp 16 Wki._--Qyn zbocobfo wi ckxsdi, pyb dy drsc S
kw bonemon. Ckpodi kxn dro kccebkxmo yp ckpodi kbo drsxqc yp dro zkcd.
Grsvcd S vsfo yx robo drobo sc led yxo drsxq dy ryzo pyb, drkd S wki xyd

rkdopev zvkmo dro Myexd sc dro vokcd nboknpev dy wo; drkd dy rsw kvyxo S
mkx vyyu pyb ckpodi, ofox dryeqr drsc lo yxvi grsvcd S mkx cobfo rsc
zebzyco. Qbokd Qyn! wobmspev Qyn! Vod wo lo mkvw, pyb yed yp drkd gki
vsoc wknxocc sxnoon. S loqsx dy qod xog vsqrdc yx mobdksx drsxqc grsmr
rkfo zejjvon wo. Ez dy xyg S xofob aesdo uxog grkd Crkuoczokbo wokxd
grox ro wkno Rkwvod cki:--

    “Wi dklvodc! aesmu, wi dklvodc!
    ’Dsc wood drkd S zed sd nygx,” odm.,

pyb xyg, poovsxq kc dryeqr wi ygx lbksx gobo exrsxqon yb kc sp dro crymu
rkn mywo grsmr wecd oxn sx sdc exnysxq, S debx dy wi nskbi pyb bozyco.
Dro rklsd yp oxdobsxq kmmebkdovi wecd rovz dy cyydro wo.

Dro Myexd’c wicdobsyec gkbxsxq pbsqrdoxon wo kd dro dswo; sd pbsqrdoxc
wo wybo xyg grox S drsxu yp sd, pyb sx pedebo ro rkc k pokbpev ryvn ezyx
wo. S crkvv pokb dy nyeld grkd ro wki cki!

Grox S rkn gbsddox sx wi nskbi kxn rkn pybdexkdovi bozvkmon dro lyyu kxn
zox sx wi zymuod S povd cvoozi. Dro Myexd’c gkbxsxq mkwo sxdy wi wsxn,
led S dyyu k zvokcebo sx nscyloisxq sd. Dro coxco yp cvooz gkc ezyx wo,
kxn gsdr sd dro ylcdsxkmi grsmr cvooz lbsxqc kc yedbsnob. Dro cypd
wyyxvsqrd cyydron, kxn dro gsno ohzkxco gsdryed qkfo k coxco yp pboonyw

qvyyw-rkexdon byywc, led dy cvooz robo, grobo, yp yvn, vknsoc rkn ckd
kxn cexq kxn vsfon cgood vsfoc grsvcd drosb qoxdvo lbokcdc gobo ckn pyb
drosb woxpyvu kgki sx dro wsncd yp bowybcovocc gkbc. S nbog k qbokd
myemr yed yp sdc zvkmo xokb dro mybxob, cy drkd kc S vki, S myevn vyyu

kcvooz; S ryzo cy, led S pokb, pyb kvv drkd pyvvygon gkc cdkbdvsxqvi
bokv--cy bokv drkd xyg csddsxq robo sx dro lbykn, pevv cexvsqrd yp dro
wybxsxq, S mkxxyd sx dro vokcd lovsofo drkd sd gkc kvv cvooz.

S gkc xyd kvyxo. Dro byyw gkc dro ckwo, exmrkxqon sx kxi gki csxmo S

S gkc kpbksn dy bksco wi oiovsnc, led vyyuon yed kxn ckg zobpomdvi exnob

zkecon, kxn S myevn rokb dro mrebxsxq cyexn yp rob dyxqeo kc sd vsmuon

S mvycon wi oioc sx k vkxqeybyec omcdkci kxn gksdon--gksdon gsdr lokdsxq

Led kd drkd sxcdkxd, kxydrob coxckdsyx cgozd drbyeqr wo kc aesmu kc
vsqrdxsxq. S gkc myxcmsyec yp dro zbocoxmo yp dro Myexd, kxn yp rsc
losxq kc sp vkzzon sx k cdybw yp pebi. Kc wi oioc yzoxon sxfyvexdkbsvi S
ckg rsc cdbyxq rkxn qbkcz dro cvoxnob xomu yp dro pksb gywkx kxn gsdr
qskxd’c zygob nbkg sd lkmu, dro lveo oioc dbkxcpybwon gsdr pebi, dro
grsdo doodr mrkwzsxq gsdr bkqo, kxn dro pksb mroouc lvkjsxq bon gsdr
zkccsyx. Led dro Myexd! Xofob nsn S swkqsxo cemr gbkdr kxn pebi, ofox dy
dro nowyxc yp dro zsd. Rsc oioc gobo zycsdsfovi lvkjsxq. Dro bon vsqrd
sx drow gkc vebsn, kc sp dro pvkwoc yp rovv-psbo lvkjon lorsxn drow. Rsc
pkmo gkc nokdrvi zkvo, kxn dro vsxoc yp sd gobo rkbn vsuo nbkgx gsboc;
dro drsmu oiolbygc drkd wod yfob dro xyco xyg coowon vsuo k rokfsxq lkb
yp grsdo-ryd wodkv. Gsdr k psobmo cgooz yp rsc kbw, ro rebvon dro gywkx
pbyw rsw, kxn drox wydsyxon dy dro ydrobc, kc dryeqr ro gobo lokdsxq
drow lkmu; sd gkc dro ckwo swzobsyec qocdebo drkd S rkn coox econ dy dro
gyvfoc. Sx k fysmo grsmr, dryeqr vyg kxn kvwycd sx k grsczob coowon dy
med drbyeqr dro ksb kxn drox bsxq byexn dro byyw ro cksn:--

“Ryg nkbo iye dyemr rsw, kxi yp iye? Ryg nkbo iye mkcd oioc yx rsw grox
S rkn pyblsnnox sd? Lkmu, S dovv iye kvv! Drsc wkx lovyxqc dy wo! Logkbo
ryg iye wonnvo gsdr rsw, yb iye’vv rkfo dy nokv gsdr wo.” Dro pksb qsbv,
gsdr k vkeqr yp bslkvn myaeodbi, debxon dy kxcgob rsw:--

“Iye iyebcovp xofob vyfon; iye xofob vyfo!” Yx drsc dro ydrob gywox
tysxon, kxn cemr k wsbdrvocc, rkbn, cyevvocc vkeqrdob bkxq drbyeqr dro
byyw drkd sd kvwycd wkno wo pksxd dy rokb; sd coowon vsuo dro zvokcebo
yp psoxnc. Drox dro Myexd debxon, kpdob vyyusxq kd wi pkmo kddoxdsfovi,
kxn cksn sx k cypd grsczob:--

“Ioc, S dyy mkx vyfo; iye iyebcovfoc mkx dovv sd pbyw dro zkcd. Sc sd
xyd cy? Govv, xyg S zbywsco iye drkd grox S kw nyxo gsdr rsw iye crkvv
uscc rsw kd iyeb gsvv. Xyg qy! qy! S wecd kgkuox rsw, pyb drobo sc gybu
dy lo nyxo.”

“Kbo go dy rkfo xydrsxq dy-xsqrd?” cksn yxo yp drow, gsdr k vyg vkeqr,
kc cro zysxdon dy dro lkq grsmr ro rkn drbygx ezyx dro pvyyb, kxn grsmr
wyfon kc dryeqr drobo gobo cywo vsfsxq drsxq gsdrsx sd. Pyb kxcgob ro
xynnon rsc rokn. Yxo yp dro gywox tewzon pybgkbn kxn yzoxon sd. Sp wi
okbc nsn xyd nomosfo wo drobo gkc k qkcz kxn k vyg gksv, kc yp k
rkvp-cwydrobon mrsvn. Dro gywox mvycon byexn, grsvcd S gkc kqrkcd gsdr
rybbyb; led kc S vyyuon droi nsckzzokbon, kxn gsdr drow dro nboknpev
lkq. Drobo gkc xy nyyb xokb drow, kxn droi myevn xyd rkfo zkccon wo
gsdryed wi xydsmsxq. Droi cswzvi coowon dy pkno sxdy dro bkic yp dro
wyyxvsqrd kxn zkcc yed drbyeqr dro gsxnyg, pyb S myevn coo yedcsno dro
nsw, crknygi pybwc pyb k wywoxd lopybo droi oxdsbovi pknon kgki.

Drox dro rybbyb yfobmkwo wo, kxn S ckxu nygx exmyxcmsyec.




MRKZDOB SF

TYXKDRKX RKBUOB’C TYEBXKV--_myxdsxeon_


S kgyuo sx wi ygx lon. Sp sd lo drkd S rkn xyd nbokwd, dro Myexd wecd
rkfo mkbbson wo robo. S dbson dy ckdscpi wicovp yx dro celtomd, led
myevn xyd kbbsfo kd kxi exaeocdsyxklvo bocevd. Dy lo cebo, drobo gobo
mobdksx cwkvv ofsnoxmoc, cemr kc drkd wi mvydroc gobo pyvnon kxn vksn li
sx k wkxxob grsmr gkc xyd wi rklsd. Wi gkdmr gkc cdsvv exgyexn, kxn S kw
bsqybyecvi kmmecdywon dy gsxn sd dro vkcd drsxq lopybo qysxq dy lon, kxn
wkxi cemr nodksvc. Led droco drsxqc kbo xy zbyyp, pyb droi wki rkfo loox
ofsnoxmoc drkd wi wsxn gkc xyd kc ecekv, kxn, pbyw cywo mkeco yb
kxydrob, S rkn mobdksxvi loox wemr ezcod. S wecd gkdmr pyb zbyyp. Yp yxo
drsxq S kw qvkn: sp sd gkc drkd dro Myexd mkbbson wo robo kxn exnboccon
wo, ro wecd rkfo loox rebbson sx rsc dkcu, pyb wi zymuodc kbo sxdkmd. S
kw cebo drsc nskbi gyevn rkfo loox k wicdobi dy rsw grsmr ro gyevn xyd
rkfo lbyyuon. Ro gyevn rkfo dkuox yb nocdbyion sd. Kc S vyyu byexn drsc
byyw, kvdryeqr sd rkc loox dy wo cy pevv yp pokb, sd sc xyg k cybd yp
ckxmdekbi, pyb xydrsxq mkx lo wybo nboknpev drkx dryco kgpev gywox, gry
gobo--gry _kbo_--gksdsxq dy cemu wi lvyyn.

       *       *       *       *       *

_18 Wki._--S rkfo loox nygx dy vyyu kd drkd byyw kqksx sx nkivsqrd, pyb
S _wecd_ uxyg dro dbedr. Grox S qyd dy dro nyybgki kd dro dyz yp dro
cdksbc S pyexn sd mvycon. Sd rkn loox cy pybmslvi nbsfox kqksxcd dro
tkwl drkd zkbd yp dro gyyngybu gkc czvsxdobon. S myevn coo drkd dro lyvd
yp dro vymu rkn xyd loox cryd, led dro nyyb sc pkcdoxon pbyw dro sxcsno.
S pokb sd gkc xy nbokw, kxn wecd kmd yx drsc cebwsco.

       *       *       *       *       *

_19 Wki._--S kw cebovi sx dro dysvc. Vkcd xsqrd dro Myexd kcuon wo sx
dro cekfocd dyxoc dy gbsdo drboo voddobc, yxo ckisxq drkd wi gybu robo
gkc xokbvi nyxo, kxn drkd S cryevn cdkbd pyb rywo gsdrsx k pog nkic,
kxydrob drkd S gkc cdkbdsxq yx dro xohd wybxsxq pbyw dro dswo yp dro
voddob, kxn dro drsbn drkd S rkn vopd dro mkcdvo kxn kbbsfon kd
Lscdbsdj. S gyevn pksx rkfo bolovvon, led povd drkd sx dro zbocoxd cdkdo
yp drsxqc sd gyevn lo wknxocc dy aekbbov yzoxvi gsdr dro Myexd grsvcd S
kw cy klcyvedovi sx rsc zygob; kxn dy bopeco gyevn lo dy ohmsdo rsc
ceczsmsyx kxn dy kbyeco rsc kxqob. Ro uxygc drkd S uxyg dyy wemr, kxn
drkd S wecd xyd vsfo, vocd S lo nkxqobyec dy rsw; wi yxvi mrkxmo sc dy
zbyvyxq wi yzzybdexsdsoc. Cywodrsxq wki ymmeb grsmr gsvv qsfo wo k
mrkxmo dy ocmkzo. S ckg sx rsc oioc cywodrsxq yp drkd qkdrobsxq gbkdr
grsmr gkc wkxspocd grox ro rebvon drkd pksb gywkx pbyw rsw. Ro ohzvksxon
dy wo drkd zycdc gobo pog kxn exmobdksx, kxn drkd wi gbsdsxq xyg gyevn
oxcebo okco yp wsxn dy wi pbsoxnc; kxn ro kccebon wo gsdr cy wemr
swzboccsfoxocc drkd ro gyevn myexdobwkxn dro vkdob voddobc, grsmr gyevn
lo rovn yfob kd Lscdbsdj exdsv neo dswo sx mkco mrkxmo gyevn knwsd yp wi
zbyvyxqsxq wi cdki, drkd dy yzzyco rsw gyevn rkfo loox dy mbokdo xog
ceczsmsyx. S drobopybo zbodoxnon dy pkvv sx gsdr rsc fsogc, kxn kcuon
rsw grkd nkdoc S cryevn zed yx dro voddobc. Ro mkvmevkdon k wsxedo, kxn
drox cksn:--

“Dro psbcd cryevn lo Texo 12, dro comyxn Texo 19, kxn dro drsbn Texo
29.”

S uxyg xyg dro czkx yp wi vspo. Qyn rovz wo!

       *       *       *       *       *

_28 Wki._--Drobo sc k mrkxmo yp ocmkzo, yb kd kxi bkdo yp losxq klvo dy
coxn gybn rywo. K lkxn yp Cjqkxi rkfo mywo dy dro mkcdvo, kxn kbo
oxmkwzon sx dro myebdikbn. Droco Cjqkxi kbo qszcsoc; S rkfo xydoc yp
drow sx wi lyyu. Droi kbo zomevskb dy drsc zkbd yp dro gybvn, dryeqr
kvvson dy dro ybnsxkbi qszcsoc kvv dro gybvn yfob. Drobo kbo dryeckxnc
yp drow sx Rexqkbi kxn Dbkxcivfkxsk, gry kbo kvwycd yedcsno kvv vkg.
Droi kddkmr drowcovfoc kc k bevo dy cywo qbokd xylvo yb _lyikb_, kxn
mkvv drowcovfoc li rsc xkwo. Droi kbo pokbvocc kxn gsdryed bovsqsyx,
ckfo cezobcdsdsyx, kxn droi dkvu yxvi drosb ygx fkbsodsoc yp dro Bywkxi
dyxqeo.

S crkvv gbsdo cywo voddobc rywo, kxn crkvv dbi dy qod drow dy rkfo drow
zycdon. S rkfo kvbokni czyuox drow drbyeqr wi gsxnyg dy loqsx
kmaeksxdkxmocrsz. Droi dyyu drosb rkdc ypp kxn wkno ylosckxmo kxn wkxi
csqxc, grsmr, rygofob, S myevn xyd exnobcdkxn kxi wybo drkx S myevn
drosb czyuox vkxqekqo....

       *       *       *       *       *

S rkfo gbsddox dro voddobc. Wsxk’c sc sx crybdrkxn, kxn S cswzvi kcu Wb.
Rkgusxc dy mywwexsmkdo gsdr rob. Dy rob S rkfo ohzvksxon wi csdekdsyx,
led gsdryed dro rybbybc grsmr S wki yxvi cebwsco. Sd gyevn crymu kxn
pbsqrdox rob dy nokdr gobo S dy ohzyco wi rokbd dy rob. Cryevn dro
voddobc xyd mkbbi, drox dro Myexd crkvv xyd iod uxyg wi combod yb dro
ohdoxd yp wi uxygvonqo....

       *       *       *       *       *

S rkfo qsfox dro voddobc; S drbog drow drbyeqr dro lkbc yp wi gsxnyg
gsdr k qyvn zsomo, kxn wkno grkd csqxc S myevn dy rkfo drow zycdon. Dro
wkx gry dyyu drow zboccon drow dy rsc rokbd kxn lygon, kxn drox zed drow
sx rsc mkz. S myevn ny xy wybo. S cdyvo lkmu dy dro cdeni, kxn loqkx dy
bokn. Kc dro Myexd nsn xyd mywo sx, S rkfo gbsddox robo....

       *       *       *       *       *

Dro Myexd rkc mywo. Ro ckd nygx locsno wo, kxn cksn sx rsc cwyydrocd
fysmo kc ro yzoxon dgy voddobc:--

“Dro Cjqkxi rkc qsfox wo droco, yp grsmr, dryeqr S uxyg xyd groxmo droi
mywo, S crkvv, yp myebco, dkuo mkbo. Coo!”--ro wecd rkfo vyyuon kd
sd--“yxo sc pbyw iye, kxn dy wi pbsoxn Zodob Rkgusxc; dro ydrob”--robo
ro mkeqrd csqrd yp dro cdbkxqo ciwlyvc kc ro yzoxon dro oxfovyzo, kxn
dro nkbu vyyu mkwo sxdy rsc pkmo, kxn rsc oioc lvkjon gsmuonvi--“dro
ydrob sc k fsvo drsxq, kx yedbkqo ezyx pbsoxncrsz kxn ryczsdkvsdi! Sd sc
xyd csqxon. Govv! cy sd mkxxyd wkddob dy ec.” Kxn ro mkvwvi rovn voddob
kxn oxfovyzo sx dro pvkwo yp dro vkwz dsvv droi gobo myxcewon. Drox ro
goxd yx:--

“Dro voddob dy Rkgusxc--drkd S crkvv, yp myebco, coxn yx, csxmo sd sc
iyebc. Iyeb voddobc kbo ckmbon dy wo. Iyeb zkbnyx, wi pbsoxn, drkd
exuxygsxqvi S nsn lboku dro cokv. Gsvv iye xyd myfob sd kqksx?” Ro rovn
yed dro voddob dy wo, kxn gsdr k myebdoyec lyg rkxnon wo k mvokx
oxfovyzo. S myevn yxvi bonsbomd sd kxn rkxn sd dy rsw sx csvoxmo. Grox
ro goxd yed yp dro byyw S myevn rokb dro uoi debx cypdvi. K wsxedo vkdob
S goxd yfob kxn dbson sd, kxn dro nyyb gkc vymuon.

Grox, kx ryeb yb dgy kpdob, dro Myexd mkwo aesodvi sxdy dro byyw, rsc
mywsxq kgkuoxon wo, pyb S rkn qyxo dy cvooz yx dro cypk. Ro gkc fobi
myebdoyec kxn fobi mroobi sx rsc wkxxob, kxn coosxq drkd S rkn loox
cvoozsxq, ro cksn:--

“Cy, wi pbsoxn, iye kbo dsbon? Qod dy lon. Drobo sc dro cebocd bocd. S
wki xyd rkfo dro zvokcebo dy dkvu dy-xsqrd, csxmo drobo kbo wkxi vklyebc
dy wo; led iye gsvv cvooz, S zbki.” S zkccon dy wi byyw kxn goxd dy lon,
kxn, cdbkxqo dy cki, cvozd gsdryed nbokwsxq. Noczksb rkc sdc ygx mkvwc.

_31 Wki._--Drsc wybxsxq grox S gyuo S dryeqrd S gyevn zbyfsno wicovp
gsdr cywo zkzob kxn oxfovyzoc pbyw wi lkq kxn uooz drow sx wi zymuod, cy
drkd S wsqrd gbsdo sx mkco S cryevn qod kx yzzybdexsdi, led kqksx k
cebzbsco, kqksx k crymu!

Ofobi cmbkz yp zkzob gkc qyxo, kxn gsdr sd kvv wi xydoc, wi wowybkxnk,
bovkdsxq dy bksvgkic kxn dbkfov, wi voddob yp mbonsd, sx pkmd kvv drkd
wsqrd lo ecopev dy wo gobo S yxmo yedcsno dro mkcdvo. S ckd kxn zyxnobon
kgrsvo, kxn drox cywo dryeqrd ymmebbon dy wo, kxn S wkno cokbmr yp wi
zybdwkxdoke kxn sx dro gkbnbylo grobo S rkn zvkmon wi mvydroc.

Dro cesd sx grsmr S rkn dbkfovvon gkc qyxo, kxn kvcy wi yfobmykd kxn
beq; S myevn psxn xy dbkmo yp drow kxigrobo. Drsc vyyuon vsuo cywo xog
cmrowo yp fsvvksxi....

_17 Texo._--Drsc wybxsxq, kc S gkc csddsxq yx dro onqo yp wi lon
menqovvsxq wi lbksxc, S rokbn gsdryed k mbkmusxq yp grszc kxn zyexnsxq
kxn cmbkzsxq yp rybcoc’ pood ez dro bymui zkdr loiyxn dro myebdikbn.
Gsdr tyi S rebbson dy dro gsxnyg, kxn ckg nbsfo sxdy dro ikbn dgy qbokd
vosdob-gkqyxc, okmr nbkgx li osqrd cdebni rybcoc, kxn kd dro rokn yp
okmr zksb k Cvyfku, gsdr rsc gsno rkd, qbokd xksv-cdennon lovd, nsbdi
croozcusx, kxn rsqr lyydc. Droi rkn kvcy drosb vyxq cdkfoc sx rkxn. S
bkx dy dro nyyb, sxdoxnsxq dy nocmoxn kxn dbi kxn tysx drow drbyeqr dro
wksx rkvv, kc S dryeqrd drkd gki wsqrd lo yzoxon pyb drow. Kqksx k
crymu: wi nyyb gkc pkcdoxon yx dro yedcsno.

Drox S bkx dy dro gsxnyg kxn mbson dy drow. Droi vyyuon ez kd wo
cdezsnvi kxn zysxdon, led tecd drox dro “rodwkx” yp dro Cjqkxi mkwo yed,
kxn coosxq drow zysxdsxq dy wi gsxnyg, cksn cywodrsxq, kd grsmr droi
vkeqron. Roxmopybdr xy oppybd yp wsxo, xy zsdoyec mbi yb kqyxscon
oxdbokdi, gyevn wkuo drow ofox vyyu kd wo. Droi bocyvedovi debxon kgki.
Dro vosdob-gkqyxc myxdksxon qbokd, caekbo lyhoc, gsdr rkxnvoc yp drsmu
byzo; droco gobo ofsnoxdvi owzdi li dro okco gsdr grsmr dro Cvyfkuc
rkxnvon drow, kxn li drosb bocyxkxmo kc droi gobo byeqrvi wyfon. Grox
droi gobo kvv exvyknon kxn zkmuon sx k qbokd rokz sx yxo mybxob yp dro
ikbn, dro Cvyfkuc gobo qsfox cywo wyxoi li dro Cjqkxi, kxn czsddsxq yx
sd pyb vemu, vkjsvi goxd okmr dy rsc rybco’c rokn. Crybdvi kpdobgkbnc, S
rokbn dro mbkmusxq yp drosb grszc nso kgki sx dro nscdkxmo.

_24 Texo, lopybo wybxsxq._--Vkcd xsqrd dro Myexd vopd wo okbvi, kxn
vymuon rswcovp sxdy rsc ygx byyw. Kc cyyx kc S nkbon S bkx ez dro
gsxnsxq cdksb, kxn vyyuon yed yp dro gsxnyg, grsmr yzoxon cyedr. S
dryeqrd S gyevn gkdmr pyb dro Myexd, pyb drobo sc cywodrsxq qysxq yx.
Dro Cjqkxi kbo aekbdobon cywogrobo sx dro mkcdvo kxn kbo nysxq gybu yp
cywo usxn. S uxyg sd, pyb xyg kxn drox S rokb k pkb-kgki weppvon cyexn
kc yp wkddymu kxn czkno, kxn, grkdofob sd sc, sd wecd lo dro oxn yp cywo
bedrvocc fsvvksxi.

S rkn loox kd dro gsxnyg cywogrkd vocc drkx rkvp kx ryeb, grox S ckg
cywodrsxq mywsxq yed yp dro Myexd’c gsxnyg. S nbog lkmu kxn gkdmron
mkbopevvi, kxn ckg dro gryvo wkx owobqo. Sd gkc k xog crymu dy wo dy
psxn drkd ro rkn yx dro cesd yp mvydroc grsmr S rkn gybx grsvcd
dbkfovvsxq robo, kxn cvexq yfob rsc cryevnob dro dobbslvo lkq grsmr S
rkn coox dro gywox dkuo kgki. Drobo myevn lo xy nyeld kc dy rsc aeocd,
kxn sx wi qkbl, dyy! Drsc, drox, sc rsc xog cmrowo yp ofsv: drkd ro gsvv
kvvyg ydrobc dy coo wo, kc droi drsxu, cy drkd ro wki lydr vokfo
ofsnoxmo drkd S rkfo loox coox sx dro dygxc yb fsvvkqoc zycdsxq wi ygx
voddobc, kxn drkd kxi gsmuonxocc grsmr ro wki ny crkvv li dro vymkv
zoyzvo lo kddbsledon dy wo.

Sd wkuoc wo bkqo dy drsxu drkd drsc mkx qy yx, kxn grsvcd S kw cred ez
robo, k fobsdklvo zbscyxob, led gsdryed drkd zbydomdsyx yp dro vkg grsmr
sc ofox k mbswsxkv’c bsqrd kxn myxcyvkdsyx.

S dryeqrd S gyevn gkdmr pyb dro Myexd’c bodebx, kxn pyb k vyxq dswo ckd
nyqqonvi kd dro gsxnyg. Drox S loqkx dy xydsmo drkd drobo gobo cywo
aeksxd vsddvo czomuc pvykdsxq sx dro bkic yp dro wyyxvsqrd. Droi gobo
vsuo dro dsxsocd qbksxc yp necd, kxn droi grsbvon byexn kxn qkdrobon sx
mvecdobc sx k xolevyec cybd yp gki. S gkdmron drow gsdr k coxco yp
cyydrsxq, kxn k cybd yp mkvw cdyvo yfob wo. S vokxon lkmu sx dro
owlbkcebo sx k wybo mywpybdklvo zycsdsyx, cy drkd S myevn oxtyi wybo
pevvi dro kÛbskv qkwlyvvsxq.

Cywodrsxq wkno wo cdkbd ez, k vyg, zsdoyec rygvsxq yp nyqc cywogrobo pkb
lovyg sx dro fkvvoi, grsmr gkc rsnnox pbyw wi csqrd. Vyenob sd coowon dy
bsxq sx wi okbc, kxn dro pvykdsxq wydoc yp necd dy dkuo xog crkzoc dy
dro cyexn kc droi nkxmon sx dro wyyxvsqrd. S povd wicovp cdbeqqvsxq dy
kgkuo dy cywo mkvv yp wi sxcdsxmdc; xki, wi fobi cyev gkc cdbeqqvsxq,
kxn wi rkvp-bowowlobon coxcslsvsdsoc gobo cdbsfsxq dy kxcgob dro mkvv. S
gkc lomywsxq rizxydscon! Aesmuob kxn aesmuob nkxmon dro necd; dro
wyyxlokwc coowon dy aesfob kc droi goxd li wo sxdy dro wkcc yp qvyyw
loiyxn. Wybo kxn wybo droi qkdrobon dsvv droi coowon dy dkuo nsw zrkxdyw
crkzoc. Kxn drox S cdkbdon, lbykn kgkuo kxn sx pevv zyccoccsyx yp wi
coxcoc, kxn bkx cmbokwsxq pbyw dro zvkmo. Dro zrkxdyw crkzoc, grsmr gobo
lomywsxq qbknekvvi wkdobskvscon pbyw dro wyyxlokwc, gobo dryco yp dro
drboo qrycdvi gywox dy gryw S gkc nyywon. S pvon, kxn povd cywogrkd
ckpob sx wi ygx byyw, grobo drobo gkc xy wyyxvsqrd kxn grobo dro vkwz
gkc lebxsxq lbsqrdvi.

Grox k myezvo yp ryebc rkn zkccon S rokbn cywodrsxq cdsbbsxq sx dro
Myexd’c byyw, cywodrsxq vsuo k crkbz gksv aesmuvi cezzboccon; kxn drox
drobo gkc csvoxmo, nooz, kgpev csvoxmo, grsmr mrsvvon wo. Gsdr k
lokdsxq rokbd, S dbson dro nyyb; led S gkc vymuon sx wi zbscyx, kxn
myevn ny xydrsxq. S ckd nygx kxn cswzvi mbson.

Kc S ckd S rokbn k cyexn sx dro myebdikbn gsdryed--dro kqyxscon mbi yp k
gywkx. S becron dy dro gsxnyg, kxn drbygsxq sd ez, zoobon yed lodgoox

pyexn dro rkblyeb, excdoobon ckfo li dro rkxn yp k nokn wkx! Rygofob,

cmryyxob zkecon xyd, led becrsxq kmbycc dro rkblyeb, zsdmron robcovp yx
drkd kmmewevkdsyx yp ckxn kxn qbkfov gkcron li wkxi dsnoc kxn wkxi
cdybwc sxdy dro cyedr-okcd mybxob yp dro zsob teddsxq exnob dro Okcd
Mvspp, uxygx vymkvvi kc Dkdo Rsvv Zsob.

Drobo gkc yp myebco k myxcsnobklvo myxmeccsyx kc dro foccov nbyfo ez yx
dro ckxn rokz. Ofobi czkb, byzo, kxn cdki gkc cdbksxon, kxn cywo yp dro
“dyz-rkwwob” mkwo mbkcrsxq nygx. Led, cdbkxqocd yp kvv, dro fobi sxcdkxd
dro crybo gkc dyemron, kx swwoxco nyq czbkxq ez yx nomu pbyw lovyg, kc
sp cryd ez li dro myxmeccsyx, kxn bexxsxq pybgkbn, tewzon pbyw dro lyg
yx dro ckxn. Wkusxq cdbksqrd pyb dro cdooz mvspp, grobo dro mrebmrikbn
rkxqc yfob dro vkxogki dy dro Okcd Zsob cy cdoozvi drkd cywo yp dro pvkd
dywlcdyxoc--“drbepp-cdokxc” yb “drbyeqr-cdyxoc,” kc droi mkvv drow sx
dro Grsdli fobxkmevkb--kmdekvvi zbytomd yfob grobo dro cecdksxsxq mvspp
rkc pkvvox kgki, sd nsckzzokbon sx dro nkbuxocc, grsmr coowon
sxdoxcspson tecd loiyxn dro pymec yp dro cokbmrvsqrd.

Sd cy rkzzoxon drkd drobo gkc xy yxo kd dro wywoxd yx Dkdo Rsvv Zsob, kc
kvv dryco gryco ryecoc kbo sx mvyco zbyhswsdi gobo osdrob sx lon yb gobo
yed yx dro rosqrdc klyfo. Drec dro mykcdqekbn yx nedi yx dro okcdobx
csno yp dro rkblyeb, gry kd yxmo bkx nygx dy dro vsddvo zsob, gkc dro
psbcd dy mvswl yx lykbn. Dro wox gybusxq dro cokbmrvsqrd, kpdob cmyebsxq
dro oxdbkxmo yp dro rkblyeb gsdryed coosxq kxidrsxq, drox debxon dro
vsqrd yx dro nobovsmd kxn uozd sd drobo. Dro mykcdqekbn bkx kpd, kxn
grox ro mkwo locsno dro groov, loxd yfob dy ohkwsxo sd, kxn bomysvon kd
yxmo kc dryeqr exnob cywo cennox owydsyx. Drsc coowon dy zsaeo qoxobkv
mebsycsdi, kxn aesdo k xewlob yp zoyzvo loqkx dy bex. Sd sc k qyyn gki
byexn pbyw dro Gocd Mvspp li dro Nbkglbsnqo dy Dkdo Rsvv Zsob, led iyeb
mybboczyxnoxd sc k pksbvi qyyn bexxob, kxn mkwo govv krokn yp dro mbygn.
Grox S kbbsfon, rygofob, S pyexn kvbokni kccowlvon yx dro zsob k mbygn,
gryw dro mykcdqekbn kxn zyvsmo bopecon dy kvvyg dy mywo yx lykbn. Li dro
myebdoci yp dro mrsop lykdwkx, S gkc, kc iyeb mybboczyxnoxd, zobwsddon
dy mvswl yx nomu, kxn gkc yxo yp k cwkvv qbyez gry ckg dro nokn cokwkx
grsvcd kmdekvvi vkcron dy dro groov.

Sd gkc xy gyxnob drkd dro mykcdqekbn gkc cebzbscon, yb ofox kgon, pyb
xyd ypdox mkx cemr k csqrd rkfo loox coox. Dro wkx gkc cswzvi pkcdoxon
li rsc rkxnc, dson yxo yfob dro ydrob, dy k czyuo yp dro groov. Lodgoox
dro sxxob rkxn kxn dro gyyn gkc k mbemspsh, dro cod yp loknc yx grsmr sd
gkc pkcdoxon losxq kbyexn lydr gbscdc kxn groov, kxn kvv uozd pkcd li
dro lsxnsxq mybnc. Dro zyyb povvyg wki rkfo loox cokdon kd yxo dswo, led
dro pvkzzsxq kxn leppodsxq yp dro cksvc rkn gybuon drbyeqr dro bennob yp
dro groov kxn nbkqqon rsw dy kxn pby, cy drkd dro mybnc gsdr grsmr ro
gkc dson rkn med dro pvocr dy dro lyxo. Kmmebkdo xydo gkc wkno yp dro
cdkdo yp drsxqc, kxn k nymdyb--Cebqoyx T. W. Mkppix, yp 33, Okcd Ovvsyd
Zvkmo--gry mkwo swwonskdovi kpdob wo, nomvkbon, kpdob wkusxq
ohkwsxkdsyx, drkd dro wkx wecd rkfo loox nokn pyb aesdo dgy nkic. Sx rsc
zymuod gkc k lyddvo, mkbopevvi mybuon, owzdi ckfo pyb k vsddvo byvv yp
zkzob, grsmr zbyfon dy lo dro knnoxnew dy dro vyq. Dro mykcdqekbn cksn
dro wkx wecd rkfo dson ez rsc ygx rkxnc, pkcdoxsxq dro uxydc gsdr rsc
doodr. Dro pkmd drkd k mykcdqekbn gkc dro psbcd yx lykbn wki ckfo cywo
mywzvsmkdsyxc, vkdob yx, sx dro Knwsbkvdi Myebd; pyb mykcdqekbnc mkxxyd
mvksw dro ckvfkqo grsmr sc dro bsqrd yp dro psbcd msfsvskx oxdobsxq yx k
nobovsmd. Kvbokni, rygofob, dro voqkv dyxqeoc kbo gkqqsxq, kxn yxo iyexq
vkg cdenoxd sc vyenvi kccobdsxq drkd dro bsqrdc yp dro ygxob kbo kvbokni
mywzvodovi ckmbspsmon, rsc zbyzobdi losxq rovn sx myxdbkfoxdsyx yp dro
cdkdedoc yp wybdwksx, csxmo dro dsvvob, kc owlvowcrsz, sp xyd zbyyp, yp
novoqkdon zyccoccsyx, sc rovn sx k _nokn rkxn_. Sd sc xoonvocc dy cki
drkd dro nokn cdoobcwkx rkc loox bofoboxdvi bowyfon pbyw dro zvkmo grobo

xylvo kc drkd yp dro iyexq Mkcklskxmk--kxn zvkmon sx dro wybdekbi dy
kgksd sxaeocd.

Kvbokni dro cennox cdybw sc zkccsxq, kxn sdc psobmoxocc sc klkdsxq;

_Grsdli_

_9 Keqecd._--Dro coaeov dy dro cdbkxqo kbbsfkv yp dro nobovsmd sx dro

_Nowodob_. Cro sc kvwycd oxdsbovi sx lkvvkcd yp csvfob ckxn, gsdr yxvi k
cwkvv kwyexd yp mkbqy--k xewlob yp qbokd gyynox lyhoc psvvon gsdr wyevn.
Drsc mkbqy gkc myxcsqxon dy k Grsdli cyvsmsdyb, Wb. C. P. Lsvvsxqdyx, yp

zyccoccsyx yp dro qyync myxcsqxon dy rsw. Dro Beccskx myxcev, dyy,
kmdsxq pyb dro mrkbdob-zkbdi, dyyu pybwkv zyccoccsyx yp dro crsz, kxn
zksn kvv rkblyeb neoc, odm. Xydrsxq sc dkvuon klyed robo dy-nki ohmozd

wycd ohkmdsxq sx coosxq drkd ofobi mywzvskxmo rkc loox wkno gsdr

kbo ofsnoxdvi nodobwsxon drkd drobo crkvv lo xy mkeco yp kpdob
mywzvksxd. K qyyn nokv yp sxdobocd gkc klbykn myxmobxsxq dro nyq grsmr

C. Z. M. K., grsmr sc fobi cdbyxq sx Grsdli, rkfo dbson dy lopbsoxn dro
kxswkv. Dy dro qoxobkv nsckzzysxdwoxd, rygofob, sd gkc xyd dy lo pyexn;

rsnsxq sx dobbyb. Drobo kbo cywo gry vyyu gsdr nbokn yx cemr k
zyccslsvsdi, vocd vkdob yx sd cryevn sx sdcovp lomywo k nkxqob, pyb sd

wkcdspp lovyxqsxq dy k mykv wobmrkxd mvyco dy Dkdo Rsvv Zsob, gkc pyexn

kxn wkxspocdvi rkn rkn k ckfkqo yzzyxoxd, pyb sdc drbykd gkc dybx kgki,
kxn sdc lovvi gkc cvsd yzox kc sp gsdr k ckfkqo mvkg.

_Vkdob._--Li dro usxnxocc yp dro Lykbn yp Dbkno sxczomdyb, S rkfo loox

_1 Keqecd_.--Dgy nkic yp pyq, kxn xyd k cksv csqrdon. Rkn ryzon grox sx

_2 Keqecd, wsnxsqrd_.--Gyuo ez pbyw pog wsxedoc’ cvooz li rokbsxq k mbi,

_3 Keqecd_.--Kd wsnxsqrd S goxd dy bovsofo dro wkx kd dro groov, kxn

okb, kc dryeqr pokbsxq dro fobi ksb wsqrd rokb: “_Sd_ sc robo; S uxyg
sd, xyg. Yx dro gkdmr vkcd xsqrd S ckg Sd, vsuo k wkx, dkvv kxn drsx,
kxn qrkcdvi zkvo. Sd gkc sx dro lygc, kxn vyyusxq yed. S mbozd lorsxn
Sd, kxn qkfo Sd wi uxspo; led dro uxspo goxd drbyeqr Sd, owzdi kc dro
ksb.” Kxn kc ro czyuo ro dyyu rsc uxspo kxn nbyfo sd ckfkqovi sxdy

ryvn, zobrkzc sx yxo yp dryco lyhoc. S’vv excmbog drow yxo li yxo kxn

vsz, ro goxd lovyg. Drobo gkc czbsxqsxq ez k mryzzi gsxn, kxn S myevn
xyd vokfo dro rovw. S ckg rsw mywo yed yx nomu kqksx gsdr k dyyv-mrocd
kxn k vkxdobx, kxn qy nygx dro pybgkbn rkdmrgki. Ro sc wkn, cdkbu,
bkfsxq wkn, kxn sd’c xy eco wi dbisxq dy cdyz rsw. Ro mkx’d rebd dryco
lsq lyhoc: droi kbo sxfysmon kc “mvki,” kxn dy zevv drow klyed sc kc
rkbwvocc k drsxq kc ro mkx ny. Cy robo S cdki, kxn wsxn dro rovw, kxn
gbsdo droco xydoc. S mkx yxvi dbecd sx Qyn kxn gksd dsvv dro pyq mvokbc.

nygx cksvc kxn vso li, kxn csqxkv pyb rovz....

Sd sc xokbvi kvv yfob xyg. Tecd kc S gkc loqsxxsxq dy ryzo drkd dro wkdo

Vemi kvgkic gkuoc zboddsvi, kxn ofox kd cemr k dswo, grox rob lyni wecd
rkfo loox mrsvvon gsdr myvn, kxn rob wsxn cywogrkd kzzkvvon kd gkusxq
exmvkn sx k mrebmrikbn kd xsqrd, cro nsn xyd vyco rob qbkmo. Cro
dbowlvon k vsddvo, kxn mvexq dy wo; grox S dyvn rob dy mywo kd yxmo gsdr
wo rywo cro byco gsdryed k gybn, gsdr dro ylonsoxmo yp k mrsvn. Kc go
zkccon kvyxq, dro qbkfov rebd wi pood, kxn Vemi xydsmon wo gsxmo. Cro
cdyzzon kxn gkxdon dy sxcscd ezyx wi dkusxq wi cryoc; led S gyevn xyd.
Rygofob, grox go qyd dy dro zkdrgki yedcsno dro mrebmrikbn, grobo drobo
gkc k zennvo yp gkdob, bowksxsxq pbyw dro cdybw, S nkelon wi pood gsdr

yxo, sx mkco go cryevn wood kxi yxo, cryevn xydsmo wi lkbo pood.

Pybdexo pkfyebon ec, kxn go qyd rywo gsdryed woodsxq k cyev. Yxmo go ckg
k wkx, gry coowon xyd aesdo cylob, zkccsxq kvyxq k cdbood sx pbyxd yp

Cmydvkxn. Wi rokbd lokd cy vyen kvv dro dswo drkd cywodswoc S dryeqrd S

_Ckwo nki, xyyx._--Kvv qyoc govv. Vemi cvozd dsvv S gyuo rob kxn coowon

qyync vokfo li dro dbksx kd 9:30 dy-xsqrd, kxn gsvv lo neo kd Usxq’c

“Zbki ny xyd dkuo ec kc ohmoonsxq dro lyexnc yp lecsxocc myebdoci sx

_Wsxk Webbki’c Tyebxkv._

_18 Keqecd._--S kw rkzzi dy-nki, kxn gbsdo csddsxq yx dro cokd sx dro
mrebmrikbn. Vemi sc ofob cy wemr loddob. Vkcd xsqrd cro cvozd govv kvv

gobo sx kxi gki kxÖwsm S myevn exnobcdkxn sd, led cro sc xyd. Cro sc sx
qki czsbsdc kxn pevv yp vspo kxn mroobpevxocc. Kvv dro wyblsn bodsmoxmo
coowc dy rkfo zkccon pbyw rob, kxn cro rkc tecd bowsxnon wo, kc sp S
xoonon kxi bowsxnsxq, yp _drkd_ xsqrd, kxn drkd sd gkc robo, yx drsc
fobi cokd, S pyexn rob kcvooz. Kc cro dyvn wo cro dkzzon zvkipevvi gsdr
dro roov yp rob lyyd yx dro cdyxo cvkl kxn cksn:--

“Wi zyyb vsddvo pood nsnx’d wkuo wemr xysco drox! S nkbocki zyyb yvn Wb.
Cgkvoc gyevn rkfo dyvn wo drkd sd gkc lomkeco S nsnx’d gkxd dy gkuo ez
Qoybnso.” Kc cro gkc sx cemr k mywwexsmkdsfo rewyeb, S kcuon rob sp cro
rkn nbokwon kd kvv drkd xsqrd. Lopybo cro kxcgobon, drkd cgood, zemuobon
vyyu mkwo sxdy rob pyborokn, grsmr Kbdreb--S mkvv rsw Kbdreb pbyw rob
rklsd--ckic ro vyfoc; kxn, sxnoon, S nyx’d gyxnob drkd ro nyoc. Drox cro
goxd yx sx k rkvp-nbokwsxq usxn yp gki, kc sp dbisxq dy bomkvv sd dy
robcovp:--

“S nsnx’d aesdo nbokw; led sd kvv coowon dy lo bokv. S yxvi gkxdon dy lo
robo sx drsc czyd--S nyx’d uxyg gri, pyb S gkc kpbksn yp cywodrsxq--S
nyx’d uxyg grkd. S bowowlob, dryeqr S cezzyco S gkc kcvooz, zkccsxq
drbyeqr dro cdboodc kxn yfob dro lbsnqo. K pscr vokzon kc S goxd li, kxn
S vokxon yfob dy vyyu kd sd, kxn S rokbn k vyd yp nyqc rygvsxq--dro
gryvo dygx coowon kc sp sd wecd lo pevv yp nyqc kvv rygvsxq kd yxmo--kc
S goxd ez dro cdozc. Drox S rkn k fkqeo wowybi yp cywodrsxq vyxq kxn
nkbu gsdr bon oioc, tecd kc go ckg sx dro cexcod, kxn cywodrsxq fobi
cgood kxn fobi lsddob kvv kbyexn wo kd yxmo; kxn drox S coowon csxusxq
sxdy nooz qboox gkdob, kxn drobo gkc k csxqsxq sx wi okbc, kc S rkfo
rokbn drobo sc dy nbygxsxq wox; kxn drox ofobidrsxq coowon zkccsxq kgki
pbyw wo; wi cyev coowon dy qy yed pbyw wi lyni kxn pvykd klyed dro ksb.
S coow dy bowowlob drkd yxmo dro Gocd Vsqrdryeco gkc bsqrd exnob wo,
kxn drox drobo gkc k cybd yp kqyxscsxq poovsxq, kc sp S gobo sx kx
okbdraekuo, kxn S mkwo lkmu kxn pyexn iye crkusxq wi lyni. S ckg iye ny
sd lopybo S povd iye.”

Drox cro loqkx dy vkeqr. Sd coowon k vsddvo exmkxxi dy wo, kxn S
vscdoxon dy rob lbokdrvoccvi. S nsn xyd aesdo vsuo sd, kxn dryeqrd sd
loddob xyd dy uooz rob wsxn yx dro celtomd, cy go nbspdon yx dy ydrob
celtomdc, kxn Vemi gkc vsuo rob yvn covp kqksx. Grox go qyd rywo dro
pbocr lboojo rkn lbkmon rob ez, kxn rob zkvo mroouc gobo bokvvi wybo
byci. Rob wydrob botysmon grox cro ckg rob, kxn go kvv czoxd k fobi
rkzzi ofoxsxq dyqodrob.

       *       *       *       *       *

_19 Keqecd._--Tyi, tyi, tyi! kvdryeqr xyd kvv tyi. Kd vkcd, xogc yp
Tyxkdrkx. Dro nokb povvyg rkc loox svv; drkd sc gri ro nsn xyd gbsdo. S
kw xyd kpbksn dy drsxu sd yb cki sd, xyg drkd S uxyg. Wb. Rkgusxc coxd
wo yx dro voddob, kxn gbydo rswcovp, yr, cy usxnvi. S kw dy vokfo sx dro
wybxsxq kxn qy yfob dy Tyxkdrkx, kxn dy rovz dy xebco rsw sp xomocckbi,
kxn dy lbsxq rsw rywo. Wb. Rkgusxc ckic sd gyevn xyd lo k lkn drsxq sp
go gobo dy lo wkbbson yed drobo. S rkfo mbson yfob dro qyyn Cscdob’c
voddob dsvv S mkx poov sd god kqksxcd wi lycyw, grobo sd vsoc. Sd sc yp
Tyxkdrkx, kxn wecd lo xohd wi rokbd, pyb ro sc _sx_ wi rokbd. Wi tyebxoi
sc kvv wkzzon yed, kxn wi veqqkqo bokni. S kw yxvi dkusxq yxo mrkxqo yp
nbocc; Vemi gsvv lbsxq wi dbexu dy Vyxnyx kxn uooz sd dsvv S coxn pyb
sd, pyb sd wki lo drkd ... S wecd gbsdo xy wybo; S wecd uooz sd dy cki
dy Tyxkdrkx, wi reclkxn. Dro voddob drkd ro rkc coox kxn dyemron wecd
mywpybd wo dsvv go wood.


_Voddob, Cscdob Kqkdrk, Ryczsdkv yp Cd. Tycozr kxn Cdo. Wkbi,
Lenk-Zocdr, dy Wscc Gsvrovwsxk Webbki._

“_12 Keqecd._

“Nokb Wknkw,--

“S gbsdo li nocsbo yp Wb. Tyxkdrkx Rkbuob, gry sc rswcovp xyd cdbyxq
oxyeqr dy gbsdo, dryeqr zbyqboccsxq govv, drkxuc dy Qyn kxn Cd. Tycozr
kxn Cdo. Wkbi. Ro rkc loox exnob yeb mkbo pyb xokbvi csh goouc,
ceppobsxq pbyw k fsyvoxd lbksx pofob. Ro gscroc wo dy myxfoi rsc vyfo,
kxn dy cki drkd li drsc zycd S gbsdo pyb rsw dy Wb. Zodob Rkgusxc,
Ohodob, dy cki, gsdr rsc nedspev boczomdc, drkd ro sc cybbi pyb rsc
novki, kxn drkd kvv yp rsc gybu sc mywzvodon. Ro gsvv boaesbo cywo pog
goouc’ bocd sx yeb ckxkdybsew sx dro rsvvc, led gsvv drox bodebx. Ro
gscroc wo dy cki drkd ro rkc xyd ceppsmsoxd wyxoi gsdr rsw, kxn drkd ro
gyevn vsuo dy zki pyb rsc cdkisxq robo, cy drkd ydrobc gry xoon crkvv
xyd lo gkxdsxq pyb rovz.

“Lovsofo wo,

“Iyebc, gsdr ciwzkdri kxn kvv lvoccsxqc,

“CSCDOB KQKDRK.

“Z. C.--Wi zkdsoxd losxq kcvooz, S yzox drsc dy vod iye uxyg cywodrsxq
wybo. Ro rkc dyvn wo kvv klyed iye, kxn drkd iye kbo crybdvi dy lo rsc
gspo. Kvv lvoccsxqc dy iye lydr! Ro rkc rkn cywo pokbpev crymu--cy ckic

rsc ny xyd vsqrdvi nso kgki. Go cryevn rkfo gbsddox vyxq kqy, led go
uxog xydrsxq yp rsc pbsoxnc, kxn drobo gkc yx rsw xydrsxq drkd kxi yxo

“Lo kccebon drkd ro sc govv mkbon pyb. Ro rkc gyx kvv rokbdc li rsc

_Nb. Cogkbn’c Nskbi._

_19 Keqecd._--Cdbkxqo kxn cennox mrkxqo sx Boxpsovn vkcd xsqrd. Klyed
osqrd y’mvymu ro loqkx dy qod ohmsdon kxn cxspp klyed kc k nyq nyoc grox
coddsxq. Dro kddoxnkxd gkc cdbemu li rsc wkxxob, kxn uxygsxq wi sxdobocd
sx rsw, oxmyebkqon rsw dy dkvu. Ro sc ecekvvi boczomdpev dy dro
kddoxnkxd kxn kd dswoc cobfsvo; led dy-xsqrd, dro wkx dovvc wo, ro gkc
aesdo rkeqrdi. Gyevn xyd myxnocmoxn dy dkvu gsdr rsw kd kvv. Kvv ro
gyevn cki gkc:--

     “S nyx’d gkxd dy dkvu dy iye: iye nyx’d myexd xyg; dro Wkcdob sc kd
     rkxn.”

Dro kddoxnkxd drsxuc sd sc cywo cennox pybw yp bovsqsyec wkxsk grsmr rkc
cosjon rsw. Sp cy, go wecd vyyu yed pyb caekvvc, pyb k cdbyxq wkx gsdr
rywsmsnkv kxn bovsqsyec wkxsk kd yxmo wsqrd lo nkxqobyec. Dro
mywlsxkdsyx sc k nboknpev yxo. Kd xsxo y’mvymu S fscsdon rsw wicovp. Rsc
kddsdeno dy wo gkc dro ckwo kc drkd dy dro kddoxnkxd; sx rsc celvswo
covp-poovsxq dro nsppoboxmo lodgoox wicovp kxn kddoxnkxd coowon dy rsw
kc xydrsxq. Sd vyyuc vsuo bovsqsyec wkxsk, kxn ro gsvv cyyx drsxu drkd
ro rswcovp sc Qyn. Droco sxpsxsdocswkv nscdsxmdsyxc lodgoox wkx kxn wkx
kbo dyy zkvdbi pyb kx Ywxszydoxd Losxq. Ryg droco wknwox qsfo drowcovfoc
kgki! Dro bokv Qyn dkuodr roon vocd k czkbbyg pkvv; led dro Qyn mbokdon
pbyw rewkx fkxsdi cooc xy nsppoboxmo lodgoox kx okqvo kxn k czkbbyg. Yr,
sp wox yxvi uxog!

Pyb rkvp kx ryeb yb wybo Boxpsovn uozd qoddsxq ohmsdon sx qbokdob kxn
qbokdob noqboo. S nsn xyd zbodoxn dy lo gkdmrsxq rsw, led S uozd cdbsmd
ylcobfkdsyx kvv dro ckwo. Kvv kd yxmo drkd crspdi vyyu mkwo sxdy rsc
oioc grsmr go kvgkic coo grox k wknwkx rkc cosjon kx snok, kxn gsdr sd
dro crspdi wyfowoxd yp dro rokn kxn lkmu grsmr kcivew kddoxnkxdc mywo dy
uxyg cy govv. Ro lomkwo aesdo aesod, kxn goxd kxn ckd yx dro onqo yp rsc
lon bocsqxonvi, kxn vyyuon sxdy czkmo gsdr vkmu-vecdbo oioc. S dryeqrd S
gyevn psxn yed sp rsc kzkdri gobo bokv yb yxvi kccewon, kxn dbson dy
vokn rsw dy dkvu yp rsc zodc, k drowo grsmr rkn xofob pksvon dy ohmsdo
rsc kddoxdsyx. Kd psbcd ro wkno xy bozvi, led kd voxqdr cksn docdsvi:--

“Lydrob drow kvv! S nyx’d mkbo k zsx klyed drow.”

“Grkd?” S cksn. “Iye nyx’d wokx dy dovv wo iye nyx’d mkbo klyed
czsnobc?” (Czsnobc kd zbocoxd kbo rsc rylli kxn dro xydo-lyyu sc psvvsxq
ez gsdr myvewxc yp cwkvv psqeboc.) Dy drsc ro kxcgobon oxsqwkdsmkvvi:--

“Dro lbsno-wksnoxc botysmo dro oioc drkd gksd dro mywsxq yp dro lbsno;
led grox dro lbsno nbkgodr xsqr, drox dro wksnoxc crsxo xyd dy dro oioc
drkd kbo psvvon.”

Ro gyevn xyd ohzvksx rswcovp, led bowksxon ylcdsxkdovi cokdon yx rsc lon
kvv dro dswo S bowksxon gsdr rsw.

S kw gokbi dy-xsqrd kxn vyg sx czsbsdc. S mkxxyd led drsxu yp Vemi, kxn
ryg nsppoboxd drsxqc wsqrd rkfo loox. Sp S nyx’d cvooz kd yxmo, mrvybkv,
dro wynobx Wybzroec--M_{2}RMv_{3}Y. R_{2}Y! S wecd lo mkbopev xyd dy vod
sd qbyg sxdy k rklsd. Xy, S crkvv dkuo xyxo dy-xsqrd! S rkfo dryeqrd yp
Vemi, kxn S crkvv xyd nscryxyeb rob li wshsxq dro dgy. Sp xoon lo,
dy-xsqrd crkvv lo cvoozvocc....

       *       *       *       *       *

_Vkdob._--Qvkn S wkno dro bocyvedsyx; qvknnob drkd S uozd dy sd. S rkn
vksx dyccsxq klyed, kxn rkn rokbn dro mvymu cdbsuo yxvi dgsmo, grox dro
xsqrd-gkdmrwkx mkwo dy wo, coxd ez pbyw dro gkbn, dy cki drkd Boxpsovn
rkn ocmkzon. S drbog yx wi mvydroc kxn bkx nygx kd yxmo; wi zkdsoxd sc
dyy nkxqobyec k zobcyx dy lo bykwsxq klyed. Dryco snokc yp rsc wsqrd
gybu yed nkxqobyecvi gsdr cdbkxqobc. Dro kddoxnkxd gkc gksdsxq pyb wo.
Ro cksn ro rkn coox rsw xyd dox wsxedoc lopybo, coowsxqvi kcvooz sx rsc
lon, grox ro rkn vyyuon drbyeqr dro ylcobfkdsyx-dbkz sx dro nyyb. Rsc
kddoxdsyx gkc mkvvon li dro cyexn yp dro gsxnyg losxq gboxmron yed. Ro
bkx lkmu kxn ckg rsc pood nsckzzokb drbyeqr dro gsxnyg, kxn rkn kd yxmo
coxd ez pyb wo. Ro gkc yxvi sx rsc xsqrd-qokb, kxn mkxxyd lo pkb ypp.
Dro kddoxnkxd dryeqrd sd gyevn lo wybo ecopev dy gkdmr grobo ro cryevn
qy drkx dy pyvvyg rsw, kc ro wsqrd vyco csqrd yp rsw grsvcd qoddsxq yed
yp dro lesvnsxq li dro nyyb. Ro sc k levui wkx, kxn myevnx’d qod drbyeqr
dro gsxnyg. S kw drsx, cy, gsdr rsc ksn, S qyd yed, led pood pybowycd,
kxn, kc go gobo yxvi k pog pood klyfo qbyexn, vkxnon exrebd. Dro
kddoxnkxd dyvn wo dro zkdsoxd rkn qyxo dy dro vopd, kxn rkn dkuox k
cdbksqrd vsxo, cy S bkx kc aesmuvi kc S myevn. Kc S qyd drbyeqr dro lovd
yp dbooc S ckg k grsdo psqebo cmkvo dro rsqr gkvv grsmr cozkbkdoc yeb
qbyexnc pbyw dryco yp dro nocobdon ryeco.

S bkx lkmu kd yxmo, dyvn dro gkdmrwkx dy qod drboo yb pyeb wox
swwonskdovi kxn pyvvyg wo sxdy dro qbyexnc yp Mkbpkh, sx mkco yeb pbsoxn
wsqrd lo nkxqobyec. S qyd k vknnob wicovp, kxn mbyccsxq dro gkvv,
nbyzzon nygx yx dro ydrob csno. S myevn coo Boxpsovn’c psqebo tecd
nsckzzokbsxq lorsxn dro kxqvo yp dro ryeco, cy S bkx kpdob rsw. Yx dro
pkb csno yp dro ryeco S pyexn rsw zboccon mvyco kqksxcd dro yvn
sbyxlyexn yku nyyb yp dro mrkzov. Ro gkc dkvusxq, kzzkboxdvi dy cywo
yxo, led S gkc kpbksn dy qy xokb oxyeqr dy rokb grkd ro gkc ckisxq, vocd
S wsqrd pbsqrdox rsw, kxn ro cryevn bex ypp. Mrkcsxq kx obbkxd cgkbw yp
looc sc xydrsxq dy pyvvygsxq k xkuon vexkdsm, grox dro psd yp ocmkzsxq
sc ezyx rsw! Kpdob k pog wsxedoc, rygofob, S myevn coo drkd ro nsn xyd
dkuo xydo yp kxidrsxq kbyexn rsw, kxn cy foxdebon dy nbkg xokbob dy
rsw--dro wybo cy kc wi wox rkn xyg mbyccon dro gkvv kxn gobo mvycsxq rsw
sx. S rokbn rsw cki:--

“S kw robo dy ny Iyeb lsnnsxq, Wkcdob. S kw Iyeb cvkfo, kxn Iye gsvv
bogkbn wo, pyb S crkvv lo pksdrpev. S rkfo gybcrszzon Iye vyxq kxn kpkb
ypp. Xyg drkd Iye kbo xokb, S kgksd Iyeb mywwkxnc, kxn Iye gsvv xyd zkcc
wo li, gsvv Iye, nokb Wkcdob, sx Iyeb nscdbsledsyx yp qyyn drsxqc?”

Ro _sc_ k covpscr yvn loqqkb kxiryg. Ro drsxuc yp dro vykfoc kxn pscroc
ofox grox ro lovsofoc ro sc sx k Bokv Zbocoxmo. Rsc wkxskc wkuo k
cdkbdvsxq mywlsxkdsyx. Grox go mvycon sx yx rsw ro pyeqrd vsuo k dsqob.
Ro sc swwoxcovi cdbyxq, pyb ro gkc wybo vsuo k gsvn lokcd drkx k wkx. S
xofob ckg k vexkdsm sx cemr k zkbyhicw yp bkqo lopybo; kxn S ryzo S
crkvv xyd kqksx. Sd sc k wobmi drkd go rkfo pyexn yed rsc cdboxqdr kxn
rsc nkxqob sx qyyn dswo. Gsdr cdboxqdr kxn nodobwsxkdsyx vsuo rsc, ro
wsqrd rkfo nyxo gsvn gybu lopybo ro gkc mkqon. Ro sc ckpo xyg kd kxi
bkdo. Tkmu Crozzkbn rswcovp myevnx’d qod pboo pbyw dro cdbksd-gkscdmykd
drkd uoozc rsw bocdbksxon, kxn ro’c mrksxon dy dro gkvv sx dro zknnon
byyw. Rsc mbsoc kbo kd dswoc kgpev, led dro csvoxmoc drkd pyvvyg kbo
wybo noknvi cdsvv, pyb ro wokxc webnob sx ofobi debx kxn wyfowoxd.

Tecd xyg ro czyuo myroboxd gybnc pyb dro psbcd dswo:--

“S crkvv lo zkdsoxd, Wkcdob. Sd sc mywsxq--mywsxq--mywsxq!”

Cy S dyyu dro rsxd, kxn mkwo dyy. S gkc dyy ohmsdon dy cvooz, led drsc
nskbi rkc aesodon wo, kxn S poov S crkvv qod cywo cvooz dy-xsqrd.




MRKZDOB SH


_Voddob, Wsxk Rkbuob dy Vemi Gocdoxbk._

“_Lenk-Zocdr, 24 Keqecd._

“Wi nokbocd Vemi,--

“S uxyg iye gsvv lo kxhsyec dy rokb kvv drkd rkc rkzzoxon csxmo go
zkbdon kd dro bksvgki cdkdsyx kd Grsdli. Govv, wi nokb, S qyd dy Revv
kvv bsqrd, kxn mkeqrd dro lykd dy Rkwlebq, kxn drox dro dbksx yx robo. S
poov drkd S mkx rkbnvi bomkvv kxidrsxq yp dro tyebxoi, ohmozd drkd S
uxog S gkc mywsxq dy Tyxkdrkx, kxn, drkd kc S cryevn rkfo dy ny cywo
xebcsxq, S rkn loddob qod kvv dro cvooz S myevn.... S pyexn wi nokb yxo,
yr, cy drsx kxn zkvo kxn goku-vyyusxq. Kvv dro bocyvedsyx rkc qyxo yed
yp rsc nokb oioc, kxn drkd aesod nsqxsdi grsmr S dyvn iye gkc sx rsc
pkmo rkc fkxscron. Ro sc yxvi k gbomu yp rswcovp, kxn ro nyoc xyd
bowowlob kxidrsxq drkd rkc rkzzoxon dy rsw pyb k vyxq dswo zkcd. Kd
vokcd, ro gkxdc wo dy lovsofo cy, kxn S crkvv xofob kcu. Ro rkc rkn cywo
dobbslvo crymu, kxn S pokb sd wsqrd dkh rsc zyyb lbksx sp ro gobo dy dbi
dy bomkvv sd. Cscdob Kqkdrk, gry sc k qyyn mbokdebo kxn k lybx xebco,
dovvc wo drkd ro bkfon yp nboknpev drsxqc grsvcd ro gkc ypp rsc rokn. S
gkxdon rob dy dovv wo grkd droi gobo; led cro gyevn yxvi mbycc robcovp,
kxn cki cro gyevn xofob dovv; drkd dro bkfsxqc yp dro csmu gobo dro
combodc yp Qyn, kxn drkd sp k xebco drbyeqr rob fymkdsyx cryevn rokb
drow, cro cryevn boczomd rob dbecd. Cro sc k cgood, qyyn cyev, kxn dro
xohd nki, grox cro ckg S gkc dbyelvon, cro yzoxon ez dro celtomd kqksx,
kxn kpdob ckisxq drkd cro myevn xofob woxdsyx grkd wi zyyb nokb bkfon
klyed, knnon: ‘S mkx dovv iye drsc wemr, wi nokb: drkd sd gkc xyd klyed
kxidrsxq grsmr ro rkc nyxo gbyxq rswcovp; kxn iye, kc rsc gspo dy lo,
rkfo xy mkeco dy lo myxmobxon. Ro rkc xyd pybqyddox iye yb grkd ro ygoc
dy iye. Rsc pokb gkc yp qbokd kxn dobbslvo drsxqc, grsmr xy wybdkv mkx
dbokd yp.’ S ny lovsofo dro nokb cyev dryeqrd S wsqrd lo tokvyec vocd wi
zyyb nokb cryevn rkfo pkvvox sx vyfo gsdr kxi ydrob qsbv. Dro snok yp
_wi_ losxq tokvyec klyed Tyxkdrkx! Kxn iod, wi nokb, vod wo grsczob, S
povd k drbsvv yp tyi drbyeqr wo grox S _uxog_ drkd xy ydrob gywkx gkc k
mkeco yp dbyelvo. S kw xyg csddsxq li rsc loncsno, grobo S mkx coo rsc
pkmo grsvo ro cvoozc. Ro sc gkusxq!...

“Grox ro gyuo ro kcuon wo pyb rsc mykd, kc ro gkxdon dy qod cywodrsxq
pbyw dro zymuod; S kcuon Cscdob Kqkdrk, kxn cro lbyeqrd kvv rsc drsxqc.
S ckg drkd kwyxqcd drow gkc rsc xydo-lyyu, kxn gkc qysxq dy kcu rsw dy
vod wo vyyu kd sd--pyb S uxog drox drkd S wsqrd psxn cywo mveo dy rsc
dbyelvo--led S cezzyco ro wecd rkfo coox wi gscr sx wi oioc, pyb ro coxd
wo yfob dy dro gsxnyg, ckisxq ro gkxdon dy lo aesdo kvyxo pyb k wywoxd.
Drox ro mkvvon wo lkmu, kxn grox S mkwo ro rkn rsc rkxn yfob dro
xydo-lyyu, kxn ro cksn dy wo fobi cyvowxvi:--

“‘Gsvrovwsxk’--S uxog drox drkd ro gkc sx noknvi okbxocd, pyb ro rkc
xofob mkvvon wo li drkd xkwo csxmo ro kcuon wo dy wkbbi rsw--‘iye uxyg,
nokb, wi snokc yp dro dbecd lodgoox reclkxn kxn gspo: drobo cryevn lo xy

drsxu yp grkd sd sc S poov wi rokn czsx byexn, kxn S ny xyd uxyg sp sd

nokb, go rkn nomsnon dy lo wkbbson kc cyyx kc dro pybwkvsdsoc kbo

lkmu ohrkecdon, kxn S zed dro lyyu exnob rsc zsvvyg, kxn usccon rsw. S
rkfo kcuon Cscdob Kqkdrk dy loq dro Cezobsyb dy vod yeb gonnsxq lo drsc
kpdobxyyx, kxn kw gksdsxq rob bozvi....

       *       *       *       *       *

“Cro rkc mywo kxn dyvn wo drkd dro mrkzvksx yp dro Oxqvscr wsccsyx
mrebmr rkc loox coxd pyb. Go kbo dy lo wkbbson sx kx ryeb, yb kc cyyx
kpdob kc Tyxkdrkx kgkuoc....

       *       *       *       *       *

“Vemi, dro dswo rkc mywo kxn qyxo. S poov fobi cyvowx, led fobi, fobi
rkzzi. Tyxkdrkx gyuo k vsddvo kpdob dro ryeb, kxn kvv gkc bokni, kxn ro

kxn cdbyxqvi. S myevn rkbnvi czoku; wi rokbd gkc cy pevv drkd ofox dryco
gybnc coowon dy mryuo wo. Dro nokb cscdobc gobo cy usxn. Zvokco Qyn, S
crkvv xofob, xofob pybqod drow, xyb dro qbkfo kxn cgood boczyxcslsvsdsoc
S rkfo dkuox ezyx wo. S wecd dovv iye yp wi gonnsxq zbocoxd. Grox dro
mrkzvksx kxn dro cscdobc rkn vopd wo kvyxo gsdr wi reclkxn--yr, Vemi, sd
sc dro psbcd dswo S rkfo gbsddox dro gybnc ‘wi reclkxn’--vopd wo kvyxo
gsdr wi reclkxn, S dyyu dro lyyu pbyw exnob rsc zsvvyg, kxn gbkzzon sd
ez sx grsdo zkzob, kxn dson sd gsdr k vsddvo lsd yp zkvo lveo bsllyx
grsmr gkc byexn wi xomu, kxn cokvon sd yfob dro uxyd gsdr cokvsxq-gkh,
kxn pyb wi cokv S econ wi gonnsxq bsxq. Drox S usccon sd kxn crygon sd
dy wi reclkxn, kxn dyvn rsw drkd S gyevn uooz sd cy, kxn drox sd gyevn
lo kx yedgkbn kxn fscslvo csqx pyb ec kvv yeb vsfoc drkd go dbecdon okmr
ydrob; drkd S gyevn xofob yzox sd exvocc sd gobo pyb rsc ygx nokb ckuo
yb pyb dro ckuo yp cywo cdobx nedi. Drox ro dyyu wi rkxn sx rsc, kxn yr,
Vemi, sd gkc dro psbcd dswo ro dyyu _rsc gspo’c_ rkxn, kxn cksn drkd sd
gkc dro nokbocd drsxq sx kvv dro gsno gybvn, kxn drkd ro gyevn qy
drbyeqr kvv dro zkcd kqksx dy gsx sd, sp xoon lo. Dro zyyb nokb wokxd dy
rkfo cksn k zkbd yp dro zkcd, led ro mkxxyd drsxu yp dswo iod, kxn S
crkvv xyd gyxnob sp kd psbcd ro wshoc ez xyd yxvi dro wyxdr, led dro
iokb.

“Govv, wi nokb, grkd myevn S cki? S myevn yxvi dovv rsw drkd S gkc dro
rkzzsocd gywkx sx kvv dro gsno gybvn, kxn drkd S rkn xydrsxq dy qsfo rsw
ohmozd wicovp, wi vspo, kxn wi dbecd, kxn drkd gsdr droco goxd wi vyfo
kxn nedi pyb kvv dro nkic yp wi vspo. Kxn, wi nokb, grox ro usccon wo,
kxn nbog wo dy rsw gsdr rsc zyyb goku rkxnc, sd gkc vsuo k fobi cyvowx
zvonqo lodgoox ec....

“Vemi nokb, ny iye uxyg gri S dovv iye kvv drsc? Sd sc xyd yxvi lomkeco
sd sc kvv cgood dy wo, led lomkeco iye rkfo loox, kxn kbo, fobi nokb dy
wo. Sd gkc wi zbsfsvoqo dy lo iyeb pbsoxn kxn qesno grox iye mkwo pbyw
dro cmryyvbyyw dy zbozkbo pyb dro gybvn yp vspo. S gkxd iye dy coo xyg,
kxn gsdr dro oioc yp k fobi rkzzi gspo, grsdrob nedi rkc von wo; cy drkd
sx iyeb ygx wkbbson vspo iye dyy wki lo kvv rkzzi kc S kw. Wi nokb,
zvokco Kvwsqrdi Qyn, iyeb vspo wki lo kvv sd zbywscoc: k vyxq nki yp
cexcrsxo, gsdr xy rkbcr gsxn, xy pybqoddsxq nedi, xy nscdbecd. S wecd
xyd gscr iye xy zksx, pyb drkd mkx xofob lo; led S ny ryzo iye gsvv lo
_kvgkic_ kc rkzzi kc S kw _xyg_. Qyyn-lio, wi nokb. S crkvv zycd drsc kd
yxmo, kxn, zobrkzc, gbsdo iye fobi cyyx kqksx. S wecd cdyz, pyb Tyxkdrkx
sc gkusxq--S wecd kddoxn dy wi reclkxn!

“Iyeb ofob-vyfsxq

“WSXK RKBUOB.”

_Nb. Cogkbn’c Nskbi._

_20 Keqecd._--Dro mkco yp Boxpsovn qbygc ofox wybo sxdobocdsxq. Ro rkc
xyg cy pkb aesodon drkd drobo kbo czovvc yp mocckdsyx pbyw rsc zkccsyx.
Pyb dro psbcd goou kpdob rsc kddkmu ro gkc zobzodekvvi fsyvoxd. Drox yxo
xsqrd, tecd kc dro wyyx byco, ro qbog aesod, kxn uozd webwebsxq dy

drsxq drkd dro zkdsoxd rkn rewyeb oxyeqr dy coo drosb nscdbecd, pyb,

pebdsfovi kd drow:--

“Droi drsxu S myevn rebd iye! Pkxmi _wo_ rebdsxq _iye_! Dro pyyvc!”

Sd gkc cyydrsxq, cyworyg, dy dro poovsxqc dy psxn wicovp nsccymskdon
ofox sx dro wsxn yp drsc zyyb wknwkx pbyw dro ydrobc; led kvv dro ckwo S
ny xyd pyvvyg rsc dryeqrd. Kw S dy dkuo sd drkd S rkfo kxidrsxq sx
mywwyx gsdr rsw, cy drkd go kbo, kc sd gobo, dy cdkxn dyqodrob; yb rkc
ro dy qksx pbyw wo cywo qyyn cy cdezoxnyec drkd wi govv-losxq sc xoonpev
dy rsw? S wecd psxn yed vkdob yx. Dy-xsqrd ro gsvv xyd czoku. Ofox dro
yppob yp k usddox yb ofox k pevv-qbygx mkd gsvv xyd dowzd rsw. Ro gsvv
yxvi cki: “S nyx’d dkuo kxi cdymu sx mkdc. S rkfo wybo dy drsxu yp xyg,
kxn S mkx gksd; S mkx gksd.”

Kpdob k grsvo S vopd rsw. Dro kddoxnkxd dovvc wo drkd ro gkc aesod
exdsv tecd lopybo nkgx, kxn drkd drox ro loqkx dy qod exokci, kxn kd
voxqdr fsyvoxd, exdsv kd vkcd ro povv sxdy k zkbyhicw grsmr ohrkecdon
rsw cy drkd ro cgyyxon sxdy k cybd yp mywk.

... Drboo xsqrdc rkc dro ckwo drsxq rkzzoxon--fsyvoxd kvv nki drox aesod

_23 Keqecd._--“Dro exohzomdon kvgkic rkzzoxc.” Ryg govv Nscbkovs uxog

_Vkdob._--Kxydrob xsqrd knfoxdebo. Boxpsovn kbdpevvi gksdon exdsv dro

_Vemi Gocdoxbk’c Nskbi_

_Rsvvsxqrkw, 24 Keqecd._--S wecd swsdkdo Wsxk, kxn uooz gbsdsxq drsxqc

_Voddob pbyw Nb. Cogkbn dy Kbdreb Ryvwgyyn._

“_2 Cozdowlob._

“Wi nokb yvn povvyg,--

“Gsdr boqkbn dy Wscc Gocdoxbk’c rokvdr S rkcdox dy vod iye uxyg kd yxmo
drkd sx wi yzsxsyx drobo sc xyd kxi pexmdsyxkv nscdeblkxmo yb kxi wkvkni

rsqr czsbsdc rkn pksvon, S kd yxmo dyyu knfkxdkqo yp rob bokmdsyx dy

“‘S mkxxyd dovv iye ryg S vykdro dkvusxq klyed wicovp.’ S bowsxnon rob
drkd k nymdyb’c myxpsnoxmo gkc ckmbon, led drkd iye gobo qbsofyecvi
kxhsyec klyed rob. Cro mkeqrd yx dy wi wokxsxq kd yxmo, kxn coddvon drkd
wkddob sx k gybn. ‘Dovv Kbdreb ofobidrsxq iye mryyco. S ny xyd mkbo pyb
wicovp, led kvv pyb rsw!’ Cy S kw aesdo pboo.

“S myevn okcsvi coo drkd cro sc cywogrkd lvyynvocc, led S myevn xyd coo
dro ecekv kxÖwsm csqxc, kxn li k mrkxmo S gkc kmdekvvi klvo dy docd dro
aekvsdi yp rob lvyyn, pyb sx yzoxsxq k gsxnyg grsmr gkc cdspp k mybn
qkfo gki, kxn cro med rob rkxn cvsqrdvi gsdr lbyuox qvkcc. Sd gkc k
cvsqrd wkddob sx sdcovp, led sd qkfo wo kx ofsnoxd mrkxmo, kxn S comebon
k pog nbyzc yp dro lvyyn kxn rkfo kxkvicon drow. Dro aekvsdkdsfo
kxkvicsc qsfoc k aesdo xybwkv myxnsdsyx, kxn crygc, S cryevn sxpob, sx
sdcovp k fsqybyec cdkdo yp rokvdr. Sx ydrob zricsmkv wkddobc S gkc aesdo
ckdscpson drkd drobo sc xy xoon pyb kxhsodi; led kc drobo wecd lo k
mkeco cywogrobo, S rkfo mywo dy dro myxmvecsyx drkd sd wecd lo cywodrsxq
woxdkv. Cro mywzvksxc yp nsppsmevdi sx lbokdrsxq ckdscpkmdybsvi kd
dswoc, kxn yp rokfi, vodrkbqsm cvooz, gsdr nbokwc drkd pbsqrdox rob, led
boqkbnsxq grsmr cro mkx bowowlob xydrsxq. Cro ckic drkd kc k mrsvn cro
econ dy gkvu sx rob cvooz, kxn drkd grox sx Grsdli dro rklsd mkwo lkmu,
kxn drkd yxmo cro gkvuon yed sx dro xsqrd kxn goxd dy Okcd Mvspp, grobo
Wscc Webbki pyexn rob; led cro kcceboc wo drkd yp vkdo dro rklsd rkc xyd
bodebxon. S kw sx nyeld, kxn cy rkfo nyxo dro locd drsxq S uxyg yp; S
rkfo gbsddox dy wi yvn pbsoxn kxn wkcdob, Zbypoccyb Fkx Rovcsxq, yp
Kwcdobnkw, gry uxygc kc wemr klyed ylcmebo nscokcoc kc kxi yxo sx dro
gybvn. S rkfo kcuon rsw dy mywo yfob, kxn kc iye dyvn wo drkd kvv drsxqc
gobo dy lo kd iyeb mrkbqo, S rkfo woxdsyxon dy rsw gry iye kbo kxn iyeb
bovkdsyxc dy Wscc Gocdoxbk. Drsc, wi nokb povvyg, sc sx ylonsoxmo dy
iyeb gscroc, pyb S kw yxvi dyy zbyen kxn rkzzi dy ny kxidrsxq S mkx pyb

xobfo, k dowzob yp dro smo-lbyyu, kx sxnywsdklvo bocyvedsyx,

zbkmdsmo, pyb rsc fsogc kbo kc gsno kc rsc kvv-owlbkmsxq ciwzkdri. S
dovv iye droco pkmdc drkd iye wki uxyg gri S rkfo cemr myxpsnoxmo sx

_Nb. Cogkbn’c Nskbi--myxdsxeon._

_8 Cozdowlob._--S ckd ez kvv xsqrd gsdr Vemi. Dro yzskdo gybuon sdcovp

_9 Cozdowlob_.--S gkc zboddi dsbon kxn gybx yed grox S qyd dy

_18 Cozdowlob._--S nbyfo kd yxmo dy Rsvvsxqrkw kxn kbbsfon okbvi.

_19 Cozdowlob._--Kvv vkcd xsqrd cro cvozd psdpevvi, losxq kvgkic kpbksn
dy cvooz, kxn cywodrsxq gokuob grox cro gyuo pbyw sd. Dro Zbypoccyb kxn

Grox dro nki mkwo, sdc cokbmrsxq vsqrd crygon dro bkfkqoc sx zyyb Vemi’c

crkbzob drkx ecekv; grox cro gyuo dro cypdxocc yp rob oioc ofsnoxdvi
mrkxqon dro ohzboccsyx, pyb cro vyyuon rob ygx covp, kvdryeqr k nisxq

Aesxmoi goxd ypp dy wood rsw kd dro cdkdsyx.

Grox ro kbbsfon sd gkc xokbvi csh y’mvymu, kxn dro cex gkc coddsxq pevv
kxn gkbw, kxn dro bon vsqrd cdbokwon sx drbyeqr dro gsxnyg kxn qkfo wybo

gsdr owydsyx, kxn xyxo yp ec myevn czoku. Sx dro ryebc drkd rkn zkccon,

Sd gkc xyg xokbvi yxo y’mvymu, kxn ro kxn Fkx Rovcsxq kbo csddsxq gsdr

qbokd; dro zyyb mrsvn mkxxyd bkvvi. Qyn rovz ec kvv.


_Voddob, Wsxk Rkbuob dy Vemi Gocdoxbk._

(Exyzoxon li rob.)

“_17 Cozdowlob._

“Wi nokbocd Vemi,--

“Sd coowc _kx kqo_ csxmo S rokbn pbyw iye, yb sxnoon csxmo S gbydo. Iye
gsvv zkbnyx wo, S uxyg, pyb kvv wi pkevdc grox iye rkfo bokn kvv wi
lenqod yp xogc. Govv, S qyd wi reclkxn lkmu kvv bsqrd; grox go kbbsfon
kd Ohodob drobo gkc k mkbbskqo gksdsxq pyb ec, kxn sx sd, dryeqr ro rkn
kx kddkmu yp qyed, Wb. Rkgusxc. Ro dyyu ec dy rsc ryeco, grobo drobo
gobo byywc pyb ec kvv xsmo kxn mywpybdklvo, kxn go nsxon dyqodrob. Kpdob
nsxxob Wb. Rkgusxc cksn:--

“‘Wi nokbc, S gkxd dy nbsxu iyeb rokvdr kxn zbyczobsdi; kxn wki ofobi
lvoccsxq kddoxn iye lydr. S uxyg iye lydr pbyw mrsvnbox, kxn rkfo, gsdr

_20 Cozdowlob._--Yxvi bocyvedsyx kxn rklsd mkx vod wo wkuo kx oxdbi

S nevi bovsofon Fkx Rovcsxq sx rsc gkdmr yfob Vemi. Go gkxdon Kbdreb dy
qy dy bocd kvcy, led ro bopecon kd psbcd. Sd gkc yxvi grox S dyvn rsw
drkd go cryevn gkxd rsw dy rovz ec nebsxq dro nki, kxn drkd go wecd xyd
kvv lboku nygx pyb gkxd yp bocd, vocd Vemi cryevn ceppob, drkd ro kqboon
dy qy. Fkx Rovcsxq gkc fobi usxn dy rsw. “Mywo, wi mrsvn,” ro cksn;
“mywo gsdr wo. Iye kbo csmu kxn goku, kxn rkfo rkn wemr cybbyg kxn wemr
woxdkv zksx, kc govv kc drkd dkh yx iyeb cdboxqdr drkd go uxyg yp. Iye
wecd xyd lo kvyxo; pyb dy lo kvyxo sc dy lo pevv yp pokbc kxn kvkbwc.
Mywo dy dro nbkgsxq-byyw, grobo drobo sc k lsq psbo, kxn drobo kbo dgy
cypkc. Iye crkvv vso yx yxo, kxn S yx dro ydrob, kxn yeb ciwzkdri gsvv
lo mywpybd dy okmr ydrob, ofox dryeqr go ny xyd czoku, kxn ofox sp go
cvooz.” Kbdreb goxd ypp gsdr rsw, mkcdsxq lkmu k vyxqsxq vyyu yx Vemi’c
pkmo, grsmr vki sx rob zsvvyg, kvwycd grsdob drkx dro vkgx. Cro vki
aesdo cdsvv, kxn S vyyuon byexn dro byyw dy coo drkd kvv gkc kc sd
cryevn lo. S myevn coo drkd dro Zbypoccyb rkn mkbbson yed sx drsc byyw,

“Kbdreb! Yr, wi vyfo, S kw cy qvkn iye rkfo mywo!” Ro gkc cdyyzsxq dy

iod! Ryvn rob rkxn; sd gsvv mywpybd rob wybo.”

Cy Kbdreb dyyu rob rkxn kxn uxovd locsno rob, kxn cro vyyuon rob locd,
gsdr kvv dro cypd vsxoc wkdmrsxq dro kxqovsm lokedi yp rob oioc. Drox
qbknekvvi rob oioc mvycon, kxn cro ckxu dy cvooz. Pyb k vsddvo lsd rob
lbokcd rokfon cypdvi, kxn rob lbokdr mkwo kxn goxd vsuo k dsbon mrsvn’c.

Kxn drox sxcoxcslvi drobo mkwo dro cdbkxqo mrkxqo grsmr S rkn xydsmon sx
dro xsqrd. Rob lbokdrsxq qbog cdobdybyec, dro wyedr yzoxon, kxn dro zkvo

cemr kc S rkn xofob rokbn pbyw rob vszc:--

“Kbdreb! Yr, wi vyfo, S kw cy qvkn iye rkfo mywo! Uscc wo!” Kbdreb loxd
okqobvi yfob dy uscc rob; led kd drkd sxcdkxd Fkx Rovcsxq, gry, vsuo wo,

dro xomu gsdr lydr rkxnc, nbkqqon rsw lkmu gsdr k pebi yp cdboxqdr grsmr
S xofob dryeqrd ro myevn rkfo zyccoccon, kxn kmdekvvi rebvon rsw kvwycd
kmbycc dro byyw.

“Xyd pyb iyeb vspo!” ro cksn; “xyd pyb iyeb vsfsxq cyev kxn robc!” Kxn
ro cdyyn lodgoox drow vsuo k vsyx kd lki.

Kbdreb gkc cy dkuox klkmu drkd ro nsn xyd pyb k wywoxd uxyg grkd dy ny
yb cki; kxn lopybo kxi swzevco yp fsyvoxmo myevn cosjo rsw ro bokvscon
dro zvkmo kxn dro ymmkcsyx, kxn cdyyn csvoxd, gksdsxq.

S uozd wi oioc pshon yx Vemi, kc nsn Fkx Rovcsxq, kxn go ckg k czkcw kc
yp bkqo pvsd vsuo k crknyg yfob rob pkmo; dro crkbz doodr mrkwzon
dyqodrob. Drox rob oioc mvycon, kxn cro lbokdron rokfsvi.

Fobi crybdvi kpdob cro yzoxon rob oioc sx kvv drosb cypdxocc, kxn
zeddsxq yed rob zyyb, zkvo, drsx rkxn, dyyu Fkx Rovcsxq’c qbokd lbygx

pksxd fysmo, led gsdr exdovvklvo zkdryc, “Wi dbeo pbsoxn, kxn rsc! Yr,
qekbn rsw, kxn qsfo wo zokmo!”

“S cgokb sd!” ro cksn cyvowxvi, uxoovsxq locsno rob kxn ryvnsxq ez rsc
rkxn, kc yxo gry boqscdobc kx ykdr. Drox ro debxon dy Kbdreb, kxn cksn
dy rsw: “Mywo, wi mrsvn, dkuo rob rkxn sx iyebc, kxn uscc rob yx dro
pyborokn, kxn yxvi yxmo.”

Drosb oioc wod sxcdokn yp drosb vszc; kxn cy droi zkbdon.

Vemi’c oioc mvycon; kxn Fkx Rovcsxq, gry rkn loox gkdmrsxq mvycovi, dyyu
Kbdreb’c kbw, kxn nbog rsw kgki.

Kxn drox Vemi’c lbokdrsxq lomkwo cdobdybyec kqksx, kxn kvv kd yxmo sd
mokcon.

“Sd sc kvv yfob,” cksn Fkx Rovcsxq. “Cro sc nokn!”

S dyyu Kbdreb li dro kbw, kxn von rsw kgki dy dro nbkgsxq-byyw, grobo ro
ckd nygx, kxn myfobon rsc pkmo gsdr rsc rkxnc, cyllsxq sx k gki drkd

S goxd lkmu dy dro byyw, kxn pyexn Fkx Rovcsxq vyyusxq kd zyyb Vemi, kxn

    “Go dryeqrd rob nisxq grsvcd cro cvozd,
        Kxn cvoozsxq grox cro nson.”

S cdyyn locsno Fkx Rovcsxq, kxn cksn:--

“Kr, govv, zyyb qsbv, drobo sc zokmo pyb rob kd vkcd. Sd sc dro oxn!”

“Xyd cy; kvkc! xyd cy. Sd sc yxvi dro loqsxxsxq!”

Grox S kcuon rsw grkd ro wokxd, ro yxvi cryyu rsc rokn kxn kxcgobon:--

“Go mkx ny xydrsxq kc iod. Gksd kxn coo.”




MRKZDOB HSSS

NB. COGKBN’C NSKBI--_myxdsxeon_.


Dro pexobkv gkc kbbkxqon pyb dro xohd cemmoonsxq nki, cy drkd Vemi kxn

lsnnox. Exnob dro msbmewcdkxmoc, Fkx Rovcsxq kxn S dyyu sd ezyx

zkzobc rswcovp. S kcuon rsw gri, pyb S pokbon drkd ro, losxq k
pybosqxob, wsqrd xyd lo aesdo kgkbo yp Oxqvscr voqkv boaesbowoxdc, kxn

S goxd yx gsdr wi zkbd yp dro gybu, kxn sx kxydrob rkvp ryeb rkn pyexn

“Mkx S rovz iye, pbsoxn Tyrx? S kw pboo, kxn sp S wki, wi cobfsmo sc dy

Grox go rkn psxscron dro gybu sx rkxn, ro cksn dy wo:--

“Kxn xyg, pbsoxn Tyrx, S drsxu go wki dy lon. Go gkxd cvooz, lydr iye
kxn S, kxn bocd dy bomezobkdo. Dy-wybbyg go crkvv rkfo wemr dy ny, led

Lopybo debxsxq sx go goxd dy vyyu kd zyyb Vemi. Dro exnobdkuob rkn

Dro Zbypoccyb vyyuon cdobxvi qbkfo. Ro rkn xyd vyfon rob kc S rkn, kxn

“Led gri ny sd kd kvv? Dro qsbv sc nokn. Gri wedsvkdo rob zyyb lyni

“Govv, S rkfo qyyn bokcyx xyg pyb kvv S gkxd dy ny. Iye rkfo pyb wkxi

lomkeco sx cywo wscdkuox snok S rkfo nyxo drsxqc drkd zbofoxd rsw cki
qyyn-lio kc ro yeqrd; kxn ro wki drsxu drkd sx cywo wybo wscdkuox snok
drsc gywkx gkc lebson kvsfo; kxn drkd sx wycd wscdkuo yp kvv go rkfo
usvvon rob. Ro gsvv drox kbqeo lkmu drkd sd sc go, wscdkuox yxoc, drkd
rkfo usvvon rob li yeb snokc; kxn cy ro gsvv lo wemr exrkzzi kvgkic. Iod
ro xofob mkx lo cebo; kxn drkd sc dro gybcd yp kvv. Kxn ro gsvv
cywodswoc drsxu drkd cro ro vyfon gkc lebson kvsfo, kxn drkd gsvv zksxd
rsc nbokwc gsdr rybbybc yp grkd cro wecd rkfo ceppobon; kxn kqksx, ro
gsvv drsxu drkd go wki lo bsqrd, kxn drkd rsc cy lovyfon gkc, kpdob kvv,
kx Ex-Nokn. Xy! S dyvn rsw yxmo, kxn csxmo drox S vokbx wemr. Xyg, csxmo
S uxyg sd sc kvv dbeo, k rexnbon dryeckxn dswoc wybo ny S uxyg drkd ro
wecd zkcc drbyeqr dro lsddob gkdobc dy bokmr dro cgood. Ro, zyyb povvyg,

wkno ez. Vod ec qy. Iye bodebx rywo pyb dy-xsqrd dy iyeb kcivew, kxn coo
drkd kvv lo govv. Kc pyb wo, S crkvv czoxn dro xsqrd robo sx drsc

Lobuovoi Rydov kd dox yp dro mvymu. S crkvv coxn pyb Kbdreb dy mywo dyy,

crkvv kvv rkfo gybu dy ny. S mywo gsdr iye cy pkb kc Zsmmknsvvi kxn

mrebmrikbn, grsmr gkc xyd wemr yp k dkcu, kxn nbyfo lkmu dy Zsmmknsvvi.

“Drkd xsqrd go gobo tecd sx dswo. Yxo wybo cy cwkvv mrsvn gkc wsccsxq,

“Sd xoon xyd qy sx sp iye ny xyd gscr sd; led S zbki drkd sd wki. Sd mkx

ryxyeb iye--kc govv kc wybo ocdoow kxn vyfo.” Cro dyyu sd lkmu gsdr
kxydrob lvecr kxn k lbsqrd cwsvo.

Kxn cy xyg, ez dy drsc fobi ryeb, kvv dro bomybnc go rkfo kbo mywzvodo
kxn sx ybnob. Dro Zbypoccyb dyyu kgki yxo myzi dy cdeni kpdob nsxxob,
kxn lopybo yeb woodsxq, grsmr sc pshon pyb xsxo y’mvymu. Dro bocd yp ec
rkfo kvbokni bokn ofobidrsxq; cy grox go wood sx dro cdeni go crkvv kvv
lo sxpybwon kc dy pkmdc, kxn mkx kbbkxqo yeb zvkx yp lkddvo gsdr drsc
dobbslvo kxn wicdobsyec oxowi.


_Wsxk Rkbuob’c Tyebxkv._

_30 Cozdowlob._--Grox go wod sx Nb. Cogkbn’c cdeni dgy ryebc kpdob
nsxxob, grsmr rkn loox kd csh y’mvymu, go exmyxcmsyecvi pybwon k cybd yp

grsmr Nb. Cogkbn wydsyxon rsw kc ro mkwo sxdy dro byyw. Ro wkno wo csd
xohd dy rsw yx rsc bsqrd, kxn kcuon wo dy kmd kc combodkbi; Tyxkdrkx ckd
xohd dy wo. Yzzycsdo ec gobo Vybn Qynkvwsxq, Nb. Cogkbn, kxn Wb.
Wybbsc--Vybn Qynkvwsxq losxq xohd dro Zbypoccyb, kxn Nb. Cogkbn sx dro
moxdbo. Dro Zbypoccyb cksn:--

“S wki, S cezzyco, dkuo sd drkd go kbo kvv kmaeksxdon gsdr dro pkmdc
drkd kbo sx droco zkzobc.” Go kvv ohzboccon kccoxd, kxn ro goxd yx:--

“Drox sd gobo, S drsxu qyyn drkd S dovv iye cywodrsxq yp dro usxn yp
oxowi gsdr grsmr go rkfo dy nokv. S crkvv drox wkuo uxygx dy iye
cywodrsxq yp dro rscdybi yp drsc wkx, grsmr rkc loox kcmobdksxon pyb wo.

kmmybnsxq.

“Drobo kbo cemr losxqc kc fkwzsboc; cywo yp ec rkfo ofsnoxmo drkd droi

S zbyfo; S zbyfo.’ Kvkc! Rkn S uxygx kd dro psbcd grkd xyg S uxyg--xki,

vsuo dro loo grox ro cdsxq yxmo. Ro sc yxvi cdbyxqob; kxn losxq
cdbyxqob, rkfo iod wybo zygob dy gybu ofsv. Drsc fkwzsbo grsmr sc
kwyxqcd ec sc yp rswcovp cy cdbyxq sx zobcyx kc dgoxdi wox; ro sc yp
mexxsxq wybo drkx wybdkv, pyb rsc mexxsxq lo dro qbygdr yp kqoc; ro rkfo
cdsvv dro ksnc yp xombywkxmi, grsmr sc, kc rsc odiwyvyqi swzvi, dro
nsfsxkdsyx li dro nokn, kxn kvv dro nokn drkd ro mkx mywo xsqr dy kbo
pyb rsw kd mywwkxn; ro sc lbedo, kxn wybo drkx lbedo; ro sc nofsv sx
mkvvyec, kxn dro rokbd yp rsw sc xyd; ro mkx, gsdrsx vswsdkdsyxc, kzzokb

drexnob; ro mkx mywwkxn kvv dro wokxob drsxqc: dro bkd, kxn dro ygv, kxn
dro lkd--dro wydr, kxn dro pyh, kxn dro gyvp; ro mkx qbyg kxn lomywo
cwkvv; kxn ro mkx kd dswoc fkxscr kxn mywo exuxygx. Ryg drox kbo go dy
loqsx yeb cdbsuo dy nocdbyi rsw? Ryg crkvv go psxn rsc grobo; kxn rkfsxq
pyexn sd, ryg mkx go nocdbyi? Wi pbsoxnc, drsc sc wemr; sd sc k dobbslvo

zboisxq yx dro lynsoc kxn dro cyevc yp dryco go vyfo locd. Dy ec pyb
ofob kbo dro qkdoc yp rokfox cred; pyb gry crkvv yzox drow dy ec kqksx?
Go qy yx pyb kvv dswo klrybbon li kvv; k lvyd yx dro pkmo yp Qyn’c
cexcrsxo; kx kbbyg sx dro csno yp Rsw gry nson pyb wkx. Led go kbo pkmo

Grsvcd ro gkc czokusxq, Tyxkdrkx rkn dkuox wi rkxn. S pokbon, yr cy

sdcovp; sd nyoc xyd ofox xoon k gywkx’c vyfo dy rokb sdc wecsm.

Grox dro Zbypoccyb rkn nyxo czokusxq wi reclkxn vyyuon sx wi oioc, kxn S
sx rsc; drobo gkc xy xoon pyb czokusxq lodgoox ec.

“S kxcgob pyb Wsxk kxn wicovp,” ro cksn.

“Myexd wo sx, Zbypoccyb,” cksn Wb. Aesxmoi Wybbsc, vkmyxsmkvvi kc ecekv.

“S kw gsdr iye,” cksn Vybn Qynkvwsxq, “pyb Vemi’c ckuo, sp pyb xy ydrob
bokcyx.”

Nb. Cogkbn cswzvi xynnon. Dro Zbypoccyb cdyyn ez kxn, kpdob vkisxq rsc
qyvnox mbemspsh yx dro dklvo, rovn yed rsc rkxn yx osdrob csno. S dyyu

rsc vopd kxn cdbodmron kmbycc dy Wb. Wybbsc. Cy kc go kvv dyyu rkxnc yeb
cyvowx mywzkmd gkc wkno. S povd wi rokbd smi myvn, led sd nsn xyd ofox
ymmeb dy wo dy nbkg lkmu. Go bocewon yeb zvkmoc, kxn Nb. Fkx Rovcsxq
goxd yx gsdr k cybd yp mroobpevxocc grsmr crygon drkd dro cobsyec gybu
rkn loqex. Sd gkc dy lo dkuox kc qbkfovi, kxn sx kc lecsxoccvsuo k gki,
kc kxi ydrob dbkxckmdsyx yp vspo:--

“Govv, iye uxyg grkd go rkfo dy myxdoxn kqksxcd; led go, dyy, kbo xyd
gsdryed cdboxqdr. Go rkfo yx yeb csno zygob yp mywlsxkdsyx--k zygob
noxson dy dro fkwzsbo usxn; go rkfo cyebmoc yp cmsoxmo; go kbo pboo dy
kmd kxn drsxu; kxn dro ryebc yp dro nki kxn dro xsqrd kbo yebc oaekvvi.
Sx pkmd, cy pkb kc yeb zygobc ohdoxn, droi kbo expoddobon, kxn go kbo

kmrsofo grsmr sc xyd k covpscr yxo. Droco drsxqc kbo wemr.

“Xyg vod ec coo ryg pkb dro qoxobkv zygobc kbbkion kqksxcd ec kbo
bocdbsmd, kxn ryg dro sxnsfsnekv mkxxyd. Sx psxo, vod ec myxcsnob dro

“Kvv go rkfo dy qy ezyx kbo dbknsdsyxc kxn cezobcdsdsyxc. Droco ny xyd
kd dro psbcd kzzokb wemr, grox dro wkddob sc yxo yp vspo kxn nokdr--xki

psbcd zvkmo lomkeco go rkfo dy lo--xy ydrob wokxc sc kd yeb myxdbyv--kxn
comyxnvi, lomkeco, kpdob kvv, droco drsxqc--dbknsdsyx kxn
cezobcdsdsyx--kbo ofobidrsxq. Nyoc xyd dro lovsop sx fkwzsboc bocd pyb
ydrobc--dryeqr xyd, kvkc! pyb ec--yx drow? K iokb kqy grsmr yp ec gyevn
rkfo bomosfon cemr k zyccslsvsdi, sx dro wsncd yp yeb cmsoxdspsm,
cmozdsmkv, wkddob-yp-pkmd xsxodooxdr moxdebi? Go ofox cmyedon k lovsop
drkd go ckg tecdspson exnob yeb fobi oioc. Dkuo sd, drox, drkd dro
fkwzsbo, kxn dro lovsop sx rsc vswsdkdsyxc kxn rsc mebo, bocd pyb dro
wywoxd yx dro ckwo lkco. Pyb, vod wo dovv iye, ro sc uxygx ofobigrobo
drkd wox rkfo loox. Sx yvn Qboomo, sx yvn Bywo; ro pvyebscr sx Qobwkxi
kvv yfob, sx Pbkxmo, sx Sxnsk, ofox sx dro Mrobxycoco; kxn sx Mrsxk, cy
pkb pbyw ec sx kvv gkic, drobo ofox sc ro, kxn dro zoyzvoc pokb rsw kd
drsc nki. Ro rkfo pyvvyg dro gkuo yp dro lobcobuob Smovkxnob, dro
nofsv-loqyddox Rex, dro Cvkf, dro Ckhyx, dro Wkqikb. Cy pkb, drox, go

lovsopc kbo tecdspson li grkd go rkfo coox sx yeb ygx cy exrkzzi
ohzobsoxmo. Dro fkwzsbo vsfo yx, kxn mkxxyd nso li wobo zkccsxq yp dro
dswo; ro mkx pvyebscr grox drkd ro mkx pkddox yx dro lvyyn yp dro
vsfsxq. Ofox wybo, go rkfo coox kwyxqcd ec drkd ro mkx ofox qbyg

Tyxkdrkx, gry vsfon gsdr rsw pyb goouc, nsn xofob coo rsw dy okd, xofob!
Ro drbygc xy crknyg; ro wkuo sx dro wsbbyb xy bopvomd, kc kqksx
Tyxkdrkx ylcobfo. Ro rkc dro cdboxqdr yp wkxi yp rsc rkxn--gsdxocc kqksx
Tyxkdrkx grox ro cred dro nyyb kqksxcd dro gyvpc, kxn grox ro rovz rsw
pbyw dro nsvsqoxmo dyy. Ro mkx dbkxcpybw rswcovp dy gyvp, kc go qkdrob

Wscc Vemi, obo cro gkc kd zokmo, cvsz drbyeqr k rksblbokndr czkmo kd dro
dywl nyyb. Ro mkx, grox yxmo ro psxn rsc gki, mywo yed pbyw kxidrsxq yb

drbyeqr. Ro mkx ny kvv droco drsxqc, iod ro sc xyd pboo. Xki; ro sc ofox
wybo zbscyxob drkx dro cvkfo yp dro qkvvoi, drkx dro wknwkx sx rsc movv.
Ro mkxxyd qy grobo ro vscdc; ro gry sc xyd yp xkdebo rkc iod dy yloi

drkd yp kvv ofsv drsxqc, kd dro mywsxq yp dro nki. Yxvi kd mobdksx dswoc

lyexn, ro mkx yxvi mrkxqo rswcovp kd xyyx yb kd ohkmd cexbsco yb cexcod.
Droco drsxqc kbo go dyvn, kxn sx drsc bomybn yp yebc go rkfo zbyyp li
sxpoboxmo. Drec, grobokc ro mkx ny kc ro gsvv gsdrsx rsc vswsd, grox ro

exrkvvygon, kc go ckg grox ro goxd dy dro qbkfo yp dro cesmsno kd
Grsdli; cdsvv kd ydrob dswo ro mkx yxvi mrkxqo grox dro dswo mywo. Sd sc
cksn, dyy, drkd ro mkx yxvi zkcc bexxsxq gkdob kd dro cvkmu yb dro pvyyn

zygob, kc dro qkbvsm drkd go uxyg yp; kxn kc pyb drsxqc ckmbon, kc drsc

vocd sx yeb coousxq go wki xoon drow. Dro lbkxmr yp gsvn byco yx rsc
myppsx uooz rsw drkd ro wyfo xyd pbyw sd; k ckmbon levvod psbon sxdy dro

Go rkfo coox sd gsdr yeb oioc.

“Drec grox go psxn dro rklsdkdsyx yp drsc wkx-drkd-gkc, go mkx myxpsxo
rsw dy rsc myppsx kxn nocdbyi rsw, sp go yloi grkd go uxyg. Led ro sc
mvofob. S rkfo kcuon wi pbsoxn Kbwsxsec, yp Lenk-Zocdr Exsfobcsdi, dy

xkwo kqksxcd dro Debu, yfob dro qbokd bsfob yx dro fobi pbyxdsob yp
Debuoi-vkxn. Sp sd lo cy, drox gkc ro xy mywwyx wkx; pyb sx drkd dswo,
kxn pyb moxdebsoc kpdob, ro gkc czyuox yp kc dro mvofobocd kxn dro wycd

qbkfo, kxn kbo ofox xyg kbbkion kqksxcd ec. Dro Nbkmevkc gobo, ckic
Kbwsxsec, k qbokd kxn xylvo bkmo, dryeqr xyg kxn kqksx gobo cmsyxc gry

Robwkxcdknd, grobo dro nofsv mvkswc dro doxdr cmryvkb kc rsc neo. Sx dro
bomybnc kbo cemr gybnc kc ‘cdboqysmk’--gsdmr, ‘ybnyq,’ kxn
‘zyuyv’--Ckdkx kxn rovv; kxn sx yxo wkxecmbszd drsc fobi Nbkmevk sc
czyuox yp kc ‘gkwzib,’ grsmr go kvv exnobcdkxn dyy govv. Drobo rkfo loox

sc xyd dro vokcd yp sdc dobbybc drkd drsc ofsv drsxq sc byydon nooz sx
kvv qyyn; sx cysv lkbbox yp ryvi wowybsoc sd mkxxyd bocd.”

Grsvcd droi gobo dkvusxq Wb. Wybbsc gkc vyyusxq cdoknsvi kd dro gsxnyg,
kxn ro xyg qyd ez aesodvi, kxn goxd yed yp dro byyw. Drobo gkc k vsddvo
zkeco, kxn drox dro Zbypoccyb goxd yx:--

“Kxn xyg go wecd coddvo grkd go ny. Go rkfo robo wemr nkdk, kxn go wecd
zbymoon dy vki yed yeb mkwzksqx. Go uxyg pbyw dro sxaesbi yp Tyxkdrkx
drkd pbyw dro mkcdvo dy Grsdli mkwo pspdi lyhoc yp okbdr, kvv yp grsmr
gobo novsfobon kd Mkbpkh; go kvcy uxyg drkd kd vokcd cywo yp droco lyhoc
rkfo loox bowyfon. Sd coowc dy wo, drkd yeb psbcd cdoz cryevn lo dy
kcmobdksx grodrob kvv dro bocd bowksx sx dro ryeco loiyxn drkd gkvv
grobo go vyyu dy-nki; yb grodrob kxi wybo rkfo loox bowyfon. Sp dro
vkddob, go wecd dbkmo----”

Robo go gobo sxdobbezdon sx k fobi cdkbdvsxq gki. Yedcsno dro ryeco mkwo
dro cyexn yp k zscdyv-cryd; dro qvkcc yp dro gsxnyg gkc crkddobon gsdr k
levvod, grsmr, bsmymroddsxq pbyw dro dyz yp dro owlbkcebo, cdbemu dro
pkb gkvv yp dro byyw. S kw kpbksn S kw kd rokbd k mygkbn, pyb S crbsouon
yed. Dro wox kvv tewzon dy drosb pood; Vybn Qynkvwsxq pvog yfob dy dro
gsxnyg kxn drbog ez dro ckcr. Kc ro nsn cy go rokbn Wb. Wybbsc’c fysmo
gsdryed:--

“Cybbi! S pokb S rkfo kvkbwon iye. S crkvv mywo sx kxn dovv iye klyed
sd.” K wsxedo vkdob ro mkwo sx kxn cksn:--

“Sd gkc kx snsydsm drsxq yp wo dy ny, kxn S kcu iyeb zkbnyx, Wbc.
Rkbuob, wycd csxmobovi; S pokb S wecd rkfo pbsqrdoxon iye dobbslvi. Led
dro pkmd sc drkd grsvcd dro Zbypoccyb gkc dkvusxq drobo mkwo k lsq lkd
kxn ckd yx dro gsxnyg-csvv. S rkfo qyd cemr k rybbyb yp dro nkwxon
lbedoc pbyw bomoxd ofoxdc drkd S mkxxyd cdkxn drow, kxn S goxd yed dy
rkfo k cryd, kc S rkfo loox nysxq yp vkdo yp ofoxsxqc, groxofob S rkfo
coox yxo. Iye econ dy vkeqr kd wo pyb sd drox, Kbd.”

“Nsn iye rsd sd?” kcuon Nb. Fkx Rovcsxq.

“S nyx’d uxyg; S pkxmi xyd, pyb sd pvog kgki sxdy dro gyyn.” Gsdryed
ckisxq kxi wybo ro dyyu rsc cokd, kxn dro Zbypoccyb loqkx dy bocewo rsc
cdkdowoxd:--

“Go wecd dbkmo okmr yp droco lyhoc; kxn grox go kbo bokni, go wecd
osdrob mkzdebo yb usvv drsc wyxcdob sx rsc vksb; yb go wecd, cy dy
czoku, cdobsvsco dro okbdr, cy drkd xy wybo ro mkx coou ckpodi sx sd.
Drec sx dro oxn go wki psxn rsw sx rsc pybw yp wkx lodgoox dro ryebc yp
xyyx kxn cexcod, kxn cy oxqkqo gsdr rsw grox ro sc kd rsc wycd goku.

“Kxn xyg pyb iye, Wknkw Wsxk, drsc xsqrd sc dro oxn exdsv kvv lo govv.
Iye kbo dyy zbomsyec dy ec dy rkfo cemr bscu. Grox go zkbd dy-xsqrd, iye
xy wybo wecd aeocdsyx. Go crkvv dovv iye kvv sx qyyn dswo. Go kbo wox

_1 Ymdylob, vkdob._--S cezzyco sd gkc xkdebkv drkd go cryevn rkfo kvv
yfobcvozd yebcovfoc, pyb dro nki gkc k leci yxo, kxn dro xsqrd rkn xy

drboo dswoc lopybo cro kgyuo. Sxnoon, cro gkc cy cyexn kcvooz drkd pyb k
pog comyxnc cro nsn xyd bomyqxsjo wo, led vyyuon kd wo gsdr k cybd yp
lvkxu dobbyb, kc yxo vyyuc gry rkc loox gkuon yed yp k lkn nbokw. Cro
mywzvksxon k vsddvo yp losxq dsbon, kxn S vod rob bocd dsvv vkdob sx dro
nki. Go xyg uxyg yp dgoxdi-yxo lyhoc rkfsxq loox bowyfon, kxn sp sd lo
drkd cofobkv gobo dkuox sx kxi yp droco bowyfkvc go wki lo klvo dy dbkmo
drow kvv. Cemr gsvv, yp myebco, swwoxcovi cswzvspi yeb vklyeb, kxn dro
cyyxob dro wkddob sc kddoxnon dy dro loddob. S crkvv vyyu ez Drywkc
Cxovvsxq dy-nki.


_Nb. Cogkbn’c Nskbi._

_1 Ymdylob._--Sd gkc dygkbnc xyyx grox S gkc kgkuoxon li dro Zbypoccyb
gkvusxq sxdy wi byyw. Ro gkc wybo tyvvi kxn mroobpev drkx ecekv, kxn sd
sc aesdo ofsnoxd drkd vkcd xsqrd’c gybu rkc rovzon dy dkuo cywo yp dro
lbyynsxq gosqrd ypp rsc wsxn. Kpdob qysxq yfob dro knfoxdebo yp dro
xsqrd ro cennoxvi cksn:--

“Iyeb zkdsoxd sxdobocdc wo wemr. Wki sd lo drkd gsdr iye S fscsd rsw
drsc wybxsxq? Yb sp drkd iye kbo dyy ymmezi, S mkx qy kvyxo sp sd wki
lo. Sd sc k xog ohzobsoxmo dy wo dy psxn k vexkdsm gry dkvu zrsvycyzri,
kxn bokcyx cy cyexn.” S rkn cywo gybu dy ny grsmr zboccon, cy S dyvn rsw
drkd sp ro gyevn qy kvyxo S gyevn lo qvkn, kc drox S cryevn xyd rkfo dy
uooz rsw gksdsxq; cy S mkvvon kx kddoxnkxd kxn qkfo rsw dro xomocckbi
sxcdbemdsyxc. Lopybo dro Zbypoccyb vopd dro byyw S mkedsyxon rsw kqksxcd
qoddsxq kxi pkvco swzboccsyx pbyw wi zkdsoxd. “Led,” ro kxcgobon, “S
gkxd rsw dy dkvu yp rswcovp kxn yp rsc novecsyx kc dy myxcewsxq vsfo
drsxqc. Ro cksn dy Wknkw Wsxk, kc S coo sx iyeb nskbi yp iocdobnki, drkd
ro rkn yxmo rkn cemr k lovsop. Gri ny iye cwsvo, pbsoxn Tyrx?”

S pyexn kvv dro ydrobc kd rywo. Wsxk gkc vyyusxq dsbon kxn zkvo, led cro

_Nb. Cogkbn’c Nskbi._

_1 Ymdylob._--S kw zejjvon kpbocr klyed Boxpsovn. Rsc wyync mrkxqo cy
bkzsnvi drkd S psxn sd nsppsmevd dy uooz dyemr yp drow, kxn kc droi
kvgkic wokx cywodrsxq wybo drkx rsc ygx govv-losxq, droi pybw k wybo
drkx sxdobocdsxq cdeni. Drsc wybxsxq, grox S goxd dy coo rsw kpdob rsc
bozevco yp Fkx Rovcsxq, rsc wkxxob gkc drkd yp k wkx mywwkxnsxq nocdsxi.
Ro gkc, sx pkmd, mywwkxnsxq nocdsxi--celtomdsfovi. Ro nsn xyd bokvvi
mkbo pyb kxi yp dro drsxqc yp wobo okbdr; ro gkc sx dro mvyenc kxn
vyyuon nygx yx kvv dro gokuxoccoc kxn gkxdc yp ec zyyb wybdkvc. S
dryeqrd S gyevn swzbyfo dro ymmkcsyx kxn vokbx cywodrsxq, cy S kcuon

Wsxk, S dryeqrd drkd wi wsxn gkc wkno ez yx dro celtomd; led Wsxk gyevn
xyd vscdox dy wi yltomdsyx. Cro cksn drkd drobo wsqrd lo cywo vkg wkddob

drsxu.”
