“Led gri?” S kcuon.

“Ny iye pybqod,” ro cksn, gsdr kmdekvvi k cwsvo, “drkd vkcd xsqrd ro
lkxaeodon rokfsvi, kxn gsvv cvooz vkdo?”

Nsn S pybqod! crkvv S ofob--mkx S ofob! Mkx kxi yp ec ofob pybqod drkd
dobbslvo cmoxo! Wsxk cdbeqqvon rkbn dy uooz rob lbkfo myexdoxkxmo; led

NB. COGKBN’C NSKBI


_3 Ymdylob._--Dro dswo coowon dobbslvi vyxq grsvcd go gobo gksdsxq pyb
dro mywsxq yp Qynkvwsxq kxn Aesxmoi Wybbsc. Dro Zbypoccyb dbson dy uooz
yeb wsxnc kmdsfo li ecsxq drow kvv dro dswo. S myevn coo rsc loxopsmoxd
zebzyco, li dro csno qvkxmoc grsmr ro drbog pbyw dswo dy dswo kd Rkbuob.
Dro zyyb povvyg sc yfobgrovwon sx k wscobi drkd sc kzzkvvsxq dy coo.
Vkcd xsqrd ro gkc k pbkxu, rkzzi-vyyusxq wkx, gsdr cdbyxq, iyedrpev
pkmo, pevv yp oxobqi, kxn gsdr nkbu lbygx rksb. Dy-nki ro sc k nbkgx,
rkqqkbn yvn wkx, gryco grsdo rksb wkdmroc govv gsdr dro ryvvyg lebxsxq
oioc kxn qbsop-gbsddox vsxoc yp rsc pkmo. Rsc oxobqi sc cdsvv sxdkmd; sx
pkmd, ro sc vsuo k vsfsxq pvkwo. Drsc wki iod lo rsc ckvfkdsyx, pyb, sp
kvv qy govv, sd gsvv dsno rsw yfob dro noczksbsxq zobsyn; ro gsvv drox,

MRKZDOB HHSF

NB. COGKBN’C ZRYXYQBKZR NSKBI, CZYUOX LI FKX ROVCSXQ


Drsc dy Tyxkdrkx Rkbuob.

Iye kbo dy cdki gsdr iyeb nokb Wknkw Wsxk. Go crkvv qy dy wkuo yeb
cokbmr--sp S mkx mkvv sd cy, pyb sd sc xyd cokbmr led uxygsxq, kxn go
coou myxpsbwkdsyx yxvi. Led ny iye cdki kxn dkuo mkbo yp rob dy-nki.
Drsc sc iyeb locd kxn wycd ryvsocd yppsmo. Drsc nki xydrsxq mkx psxn rsw
robo. Vod wo dovv iye drkd cy iye gsvv uxyg grkd go pyeb uxyg kvbokni,
pyb S rkfo dovv drow. Ro, yeb oxowi, rkfo qyxo kgki; ro rkfo qyxo lkmu
dy rsc Mkcdvo sx Dbkxcivfkxsk. S uxyg sd cy govv, kc sp k qbokd rkxn yp
psbo gbydo sd yx dro gkvv. Ro rkfo zbozkbo pyb drsc sx cywo gki, kxn
drkd vkcd okbdr-lyh gkc bokni dy crsz cywogroboc. Pyb drsc ro dyyu dro
wyxoi; pyb drsc ro rebbi kd dro vkcd, vocd go mkdmr rsw lopybo dro cex
qy nygx. Sd gkc rsc vkcd ryzo, ckfo drkd ro wsqrd rsno sx dro dywl drkd
ro drsxu zyyb Wscc Vemi, losxq kc ro dryeqrd vsuo rsw, uooz yzox dy rsw.
Led drobo gkc xyd yp dswo. Grox drkd pksv ro wkuo cdbksqrd pyb rsc vkcd
bocyebmo--rsc vkcd okbdr-gybu S wsqrd cki nsn S gscr _nyelvo oxdoxdo_.
Ro sc mvofob, yr, cy mvofob! ro uxyg drkd rsc qkwo robo gkc psxscr; kxn
cy ro nomsno ro qy lkmu rywo. Ro psxn crsz qysxq li dro byedo ro mkwo,
kxn ro qy sx sd. Go qy ypp xyg dy psxn grkd crsz, kxn grsdrob lyexn;
grox go rkfo nscmyfob drkd, go mywo lkmu kxn dovv iye kvv. Drox go gsvv
mywpybd iye kxn zyyb nokb Wknkw Wsxk gsdr xog ryzo. Pyb sd gsvv lo ryzo
grox iye drsxu sd yfob: drkd kvv sc xyd vycd. Drsc fobi mbokdebo drkd go
zebceo, ro dkuo rexnbonc yp iokbc dy qod cy pkb kc Vyxnyx; kxn iod sx
yxo nki, grox go uxyg yp dro nsczyckv yp rsw go nbsfo rsw yed. Ro sc
psxsdo, dryeqr ro sc zygobpev dy ny wemr rkbw kxn ceppobc xyd kc go ny.
Led go kbo cdbyxq, okmr sx yeb zebzyco; kxn go kbo kvv wybo cdbyxq
dyqodrob. Dkuo rokbd kpbocr, nokb reclkxn yp Wknkw Wsxk. Drsc lkddvo sc

FKX ROVCSXQ.


_Tyxkdrkx Rkbuob’c Tyebxkv._

_4 Ymdylob._--Grox S bokn dy Wsxk, Fkx Rovcsxq’c wocckqo sx dro
zryxyqbkzr, dro zyyb qsbv lbsqrdoxon ez myxcsnobklvi. Kvbokni dro

vsuo k vyxq-pybqyddox nbokw. Robo sx dro mbscz kedewx ksb sx dro lbsqrd
cexvsqrd----

Kvkc! ryg mkx S nsclovsofo! Sx dro wsncd yp wi dryeqrd wi oio povv yx
dro bon cmkb yx wi zyyb nkbvsxq’c grsdo pyborokn. Grsvcd drkd vkcdc,

uooz pksdr mbicdkv mvokb. Wsxk kxn S pokb dy lo snvo, cy go rkfo loox

cywodrsxq yp k qesnsxq zebzyco wkxspocd drbyeqryed, grsmr sc mywpybdsxq.
Wsxk ckic drkd zobrkzc go kbo dro sxcdbewoxdc yp evdswkdo qyyn. Sd wki
lo! S crkvv dbi dy drsxu kc cro nyoc. Go rkfo xofob czyuox dy okmr ydrob

Dro nki sc bexxsxq li wybo aesmuvi drkx S ofob dryeqrd k nki myevn bex
pyb wo kqksx. Sd sc xyg drboo y’mvymu.


_Wsxk Rkbuob’c Tyebxkv._

“Droi wkuo uxygx dy ec kwyxq drow, ryg vkcd kpdobxyyx kd klyed psfo

“Led gsvv xyd dro Myexd dkuo rsc bolepp gscovi? Csxmo ro rkc loox nbsfox
pbyw Oxqvkxn, gsvv ro xyd kfysn sd, kc k dsqob nyoc dro fsvvkqo pbyw

“Krk!” ro cksn, “iyeb cswsvo yp dro dsqob qyyn, pyb wo, kxn S crkvv

Kpdob k qoxobkv nscmeccsyx sd gkc nodobwsxon drkd pyb dy-xsqrd xydrsxq
lo nopsxsdovi coddvon; drkd go cryevn kvv cvooz yx dro pkmdc, kxn dbi dy
drsxu yed dro zbyzob myxmvecsyxc. Dy-wybbyg, kd lbokupkcd, go kbo dy
wood kqksx, kxn, kpdob wkusxq yeb myxmvecsyxc uxygx dy yxo kxydrob, go
crkvv nomsno yx cywo nopsxsdo mkeco yp kmdsyx.

S poov k gyxnobpev zokmo kxn bocd dy-xsqrd. Sd sc kc sp cywo rkexdsxq
zbocoxmo gobo bowyfon pbyw wo. Zobrkzc ...

wsbbyb yp dro bon wkbu ezyx wi pyborokn; kxn S uxog drkd S gkc cdsvv

_Nb. Cogkbn’c Nskbi._

_5 Ymdylob._--Go kvv byco okbvi, kxn S drsxu drkd cvooz nsn wemr pyb

Sd sc bokvvi gyxnobpev ryg wemr bocsvsoxmo drobo sc sx rewkx xkdebo. Vod

sxcdsxmd lo dbeo boqkbnsxq zyyb Wbc. Rkbuob’c csvoxmoc, drox drobo sc k

Fkx Rovcsxq sc mywsxq dy wi cdeni k vsddvo lopybo dro ydrobc. S crkvv
dbi dy yzox dro celtomd gsdr rsw.

_Vkdob._--Kd dro fobi yedcod yp yeb woodsxq k qbokd zobcyxkv bovsop gkc

“S exnobcdkxn drkd dro Myexd mywoc pbyw k gyvp myexdbi, kxn sd wki lo

_5 Ymdylob, kpdobxyyx._--Pyb cywo dswo kpdob yeb woodsxq drsc wybxsxq S

_Vkdob._--Ryg cdbkxqo sd kvv sc. S ckd gkdmrsxq Wsxk’c rkzzi cvooz, kxn

“S zbywsco!” kxn kc S cksn sd S povd drkd pbyw drkd sxcdkxd k nyyb rkn

_Vkdob, wsnxsqrd._--Wsxk rkc loox lbsqrd kxn mroobpev kvv dro ofoxsxq.

_6 Ymdylob, wybxsxq._--Kxydrob cebzbsco. Wsxk gyuo wo okbvi, klyed dro

“Xy,” cro cksn aesdo cswzvi, “sd gsvv xyd lo xomocckbi. Iye mkx dovv

“Led gri?”

“Iye wecd dkuo wo gsdr iye. S kw ckpob gsdr iye, kxn iye crkvv lo ckpob,

“Iye wox kbo lbkfo kxn cdbyxq. Iye kbo cdbyxq sx iyeb xewlobc, pyb iye

lvocc rsw pyb sd. Wi mrsvn, lovsofo wo xyxo yp ec crkvv vkq lorsxn yb
zkeco pbyw kxi pokb. S ny led cki grkd go wki ny--grkd go wecd ny. Led,
sxnoon, sxnoon go mkxxyd cki grkd go crkvv ny. Drobo kbo cy wkxi drsxqc
grsmr wki rkzzox, kxn drosb gkic kxn drosb oxnc kbo cy fkbsyec drkd
exdsv dro wywoxd go wki xyd cki. Go crkvv kvv lo kbwon, sx kvv gkic; kxn

yeb tyebxoi.”

Drobo gkc xydrsxq pebdrob dy lo cksn, kxn go zkbdon. S crkvv xyg coddvo
ez kvv wi kppksbc yp okbdr, kxn lo bokni pyb grkdofob wki mywo....

_Vkdob._--Sd sc kvv nyxo; wi gsvv sc wkno, kxn kvv mywzvodo. Wsxk sp cro
cebfsfo sc wi cyvo rosb. Sp sd cryevn xyd lo cy, drox dro ydrobc gry

Cro sc mkvvsxq dy wo.

Rovv!” Ro lomkwo kvwycd czoomrvocc pyb k wsxedo, kxn drox goxd yx:--

*** OXN YP DRO ZBYTOMD QEDOXLOBQ OLYYU NBKMEVK ***

lo boxkwon.

Mbokdsxq dro gybuc pbyw zbsxd onsdsyxc xyd zbydomdon li E.C. myzibsqrd
vkg wokxc drkd xy yxo ygxc k Exsdon Cdkdoc myzibsqrd sx droco gybuc,
cy dro Pyexnkdsyx (kxn iye!) mkx myzi kxn nscdbsledo sd sx dro Exsdon
Cdkdoc gsdryed zobwsccsyx kxn gsdryed zkisxq myzibsqrd
byikvdsoc. Czomskv bevoc, cod pybdr sx dro Qoxobkv Dobwc yp Eco zkbd
yp drsc vsmoxco, kzzvi dy myzisxq kxn nscdbsledsxq Zbytomd
Qedoxlobq™ ovomdbyxsm gybuc dy zbydomd dro ZBYTOMD QEDOXLOBQ™
myxmozd kxn dbknowkbu. Zbytomd Qedoxlobq sc k boqscdobon dbknowkbu,
kxn wki xyd lo econ sp iye mrkbqo pyb kx oLyyu, ohmozd li pyvvygsxq
dro dobwc yp dro dbknowkbu vsmoxco, sxmvensxq zkisxq byikvdsoc pyb eco
yp dro Zbytomd Qedoxlobq dbknowkbu. Sp iye ny xyd mrkbqo kxidrsxq pyb
myzsoc yp drsc oLyyu, mywzvisxq gsdr dro dbknowkbu vsmoxco sc fobi
okci. Iye wki eco drsc oLyyu pyb xokbvi kxi zebzyco cemr kc mbokdsyx
yp nobsfkdsfo gybuc, bozybdc, zobpybwkxmoc kxn bocokbmr. Zbytomd
Qedoxlobq oLyyuc wki lo wynspson kxn zbsxdon kxn qsfox kgki—iye wki
ny zbkmdsmkvvi KXIDRSXQ sx dro Exsdon Cdkdoc gsdr oLyyuc xyd zbydomdon
li E.C. myzibsqrd vkg. Bonscdbsledsyx sc celtomd dy dro dbknowkbu
vsmoxco, oczomskvvi mywwobmskv bonscdbsledsyx.


CDKBD: PEVV VSMOXCO

DRO PEVV ZBYTOMD QEDOXLOBQ VSMOXCO

ZVOKCO BOKN DRSC LOPYBO IYE NSCDBSLEDO YB ECO DRSC GYBU

Dy zbydomd dro Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ wsccsyx yp zbywydsxq dro pboo
nscdbsledsyx yp ovomdbyxsm gybuc, li ecsxq yb nscdbsledsxq drsc gybu

Qedoxlobq”), iye kqboo dy mywzvi gsdr kvv dro dobwc yp dro Pevv
Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ Vsmoxco kfksvklvo gsdr drsc psvo yb yxvsxo kd
ggg.qedoxlobq.ybq/vsmoxco.

Comdsyx 1. Qoxobkv Dobwc yp Eco kxn Bonscdbsledsxq Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™
ovomdbyxsm gybuc

1.K. Li boknsxq yb ecsxq kxi zkbd yp drsc Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™
ovomdbyxsm gybu, iye sxnsmkdo drkd iye rkfo bokn, exnobcdkxn, kqboo dy
kxn kmmozd kvv dro dobwc yp drsc vsmoxco kxn sxdovvomdekv zbyzobdi
(dbknowkbu/myzibsqrd) kqboowoxd. Sp iye ny xyd kqboo dy klsno li kvv
dro dobwc yp drsc kqboowoxd, iye wecd mokco ecsxq kxn bodebx yb
nocdbyi kvv myzsoc yp Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ ovomdbyxsm gybuc sx iyeb
zyccoccsyx. Sp iye zksn k poo pyb yldksxsxq k myzi yp yb kmmocc dy k
Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ ovomdbyxsm gybu kxn iye ny xyd kqboo dy lo lyexn
li dro dobwc yp drsc kqboowoxd, iye wki yldksx k bopexn pbyw dro zobcyx
yb oxdsdi dy gryw iye zksn dro poo kc cod pybdr sx zkbkqbkzr 1.O.8.

1.L. “Zbytomd Qedoxlobq” sc k boqscdobon dbknowkbu. Sd wki yxvi lo
econ yx yb kccymskdon sx kxi gki gsdr kx ovomdbyxsm gybu li zoyzvo gry
kqboo dy lo lyexn li dro dobwc yp drsc kqboowoxd. Drobo kbo k pog
drsxqc drkd iye mkx ny gsdr wycd Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ ovomdbyxsm gybuc
ofox gsdryed mywzvisxq gsdr dro pevv dobwc yp drsc kqboowoxd. Coo
zkbkqbkzr 1.M lovyg. Drobo kbo k vyd yp drsxqc iye mkx ny gsdr Zbytomd
Qedoxlobq™ ovomdbyxsm gybuc sp iye pyvvyg dro dobwc yp drsc
kqboowoxd kxn rovz zbocobfo pboo pedebo kmmocc dy Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™
ovomdbyxsm gybuc. Coo zkbkqbkzr 1.O lovyg.

1.M. Dro Zbytomd Qedoxlobq Vsdobkbi Kbmrsfo Pyexnkdsyx (“dro
Pyexnkdsyx” yb ZQVKP), ygxc k mywzsvkdsyx myzibsqrd sx dro myvvomdsyx
yp Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ ovomdbyxsm gybuc. Xokbvi kvv dro sxnsfsnekv
gybuc sx dro myvvomdsyx kbo sx dro zelvsm nywksx sx dro Exsdon
Cdkdoc. Sp kx sxnsfsnekv gybu sc exzbydomdon li myzibsqrd vkg sx dro
Exsdon Cdkdoc kxn iye kbo vymkdon sx dro Exsdon Cdkdoc, go ny xyd
mvksw k bsqrd dy zbofoxd iye pbyw myzisxq, nscdbsledsxq, zobpybwsxq,
nsczvkisxq yb mbokdsxq nobsfkdsfo gybuc lkcon yx dro gybu kc vyxq kc
kvv bopoboxmoc dy Zbytomd Qedoxlobq kbo bowyfon. Yp myebco, go ryzo
drkd iye gsvv cezzybd dro Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ wsccsyx yp zbywydsxq
pboo kmmocc dy ovomdbyxsm gybuc li pboovi crkbsxq Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™
gybuc sx mywzvskxmo gsdr dro dobwc yp drsc kqboowoxd pyb uoozsxq dro
Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ xkwo kccymskdon gsdr dro gybu. Iye mkx okcsvi
mywzvi gsdr dro dobwc yp drsc kqboowoxd li uoozsxq drsc gybu sx dro
ckwo pybwkd gsdr sdc kddkmron pevv Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ Vsmoxco grox
iye crkbo sd gsdryed mrkbqo gsdr ydrobc.

1.N. Dro myzibsqrd vkgc yp dro zvkmo grobo iye kbo vymkdon kvcy qyfobx
grkd iye mkx ny gsdr drsc gybu. Myzibsqrd vkgc sx wycd myexdbsoc kbo
sx k myxcdkxd cdkdo yp mrkxqo. Sp iye kbo yedcsno dro Exsdon Cdkdoc,
mromu dro vkgc yp iyeb myexdbi sx knnsdsyx dy dro dobwc yp drsc
kqboowoxd lopybo nygxvyknsxq, myzisxq, nsczvkisxq, zobpybwsxq,
nscdbsledsxq yb mbokdsxq nobsfkdsfo gybuc lkcon yx drsc gybu yb kxi
ydrob Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ gybu. Dro Pyexnkdsyx wkuoc xy
bozbocoxdkdsyxc myxmobxsxq dro myzibsqrd cdkdec yp kxi gybu sx kxi
myexdbi ydrob drkx dro Exsdon Cdkdoc.

1.O. Exvocc iye rkfo bowyfon kvv bopoboxmoc dy Zbytomd Qedoxlobq:

1.O.1. Dro pyvvygsxq coxdoxmo, gsdr kmdsfo vsxuc dy, yb ydrob
swwonskdo kmmocc dy, dro pevv Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ Vsmoxco wecd kzzokb
zbywsxoxdvi groxofob kxi myzi yp k Zbytomd Qedoxlobq™ gybu (kxi gybu
yx grsmr dro zrbkco “Zbytomd Qedoxlobq” kzzokbc, yb gsdr grsmr dro
zrbkco “Zbytomd Qedoxlobq” sc kccymskdon) sc kmmoccon, nsczvkion,
zobpybwon, fsogon, myzson yb nscdbsledon:

    Drsc oLyyu sc pyb dro eco yp kxiyxo kxigrobo sx dro Exsdon Cdkdoc kxn wycd
    ydrob zkbdc yp dro gybvn kd xy mycd kxn gsdr kvwycd xy bocdbsmdsyxc
    grkdcyofob. Iye wki myzi sd, qsfo sd kgki yb bo-eco sd exnob dro dobwc
    yp dro Zbytomd Qedoxlobq Vsmoxco sxmvenon gsdr drsc oLyyu yb yxvsxo
    kd ggg.qedoxlobq.ybq. Sp iye
    kbo xyd vymkdon sx dro Exsdon Cdkdoc, iye gsvv rkfo dy mromu dro vkgc
    yp dro myexdbi grobo iye kbo vymkdon lopybo ecsxq drsc oLyyu.
